Changshu 97

▲ Deserters Rob Near the City: After the troops stationed in Changshu were withdrawn, more than a dozen deserters gathered together and arbitrarily looted in various villages. On the morning of the 16th, around 2:00 AM, eleven deserters wearing uniforms without insignias arrived at the Xiao Maojia Shen Tong Fang area, about five li outside the North Water Gate of the city. They first fired their rifles to intimidate the residents. The partners inside scattered upon hearing the sounds. The deserters then arbitrarily looted everything within the Fang, taking all the foreign goods and women's jewelry. Afterward, they went to Gujiawan Lusanjiu's house near the Xingfu Temple at the North Dry Gate to loot. They dispersed at dawn. After receiving the report, the Public Security Bureau dispatched a security team, but they did not return to the city by evening.

▲ Provincial Committee Investigates Enemy Grain Supply Case: This county has fertile land and was originally a rice-producing area. Neighboring areas such as Shanghai, Chongming, and Haimen must come to Changshu every year to purchase food, amounting to tens of thousands of shi. The county government only needs to have a formal transport permit from these counties to allow the rice to pass. This year, since the January 28th Incident, the enemy, due to a shortage of food, colluded with merchants to purchase rice at high prices in the interior. At that time, this county was ordered by the military to prepare for long-term resistance, requiring the county to reserve enough domestic rice to supply 100,000 soldiers for a year. Therefore, even with permits from neighboring counties, exports were not allowed. However, treacherous merchants, tempted by huge profits, secretly came from Haimen and Chongming counties to purchase rice. Several ships carrying thousands of shi of rice were intercepted successively at ports and the Luyuan area. Subsequently, someone reported to the authorities, suspecting certain merchants of supplying grain to the enemy. At the same time, the Chongming county government was also bombarded with telegrams from the county's citizens to the provincial authorities, accusing the county government of issuing permits and aiding the enemy. They requested an investigation. At the time, the provincial authorities were unable to investigate immediately due to the military situation. Now, to clarify the truth, the Civil Affairs Department dispatched Wu Zezhong, a committee member, to investigate and verify the matter. After receiving the order, Committee Member Wu arrived in Changshu on the 15th of this month to secretly investigate the rice purchases made by the county. He went to the county government to review all the case files. It is said that Committee Member Wu will stay in Changshu for one or two days and then cross the river to Chongming County for a secret investigation.

Wuxi 98

▲ Xinji Steamboat Robbed Yesterday Morning: Robbery cases in this county are more frequent than in other counties. The Shanghai and Wuxi newspapers cannot record them all. The public security authorities rarely solve them, so the trend of theft is rampant. Several alarms occur in one night, causing great unease for the police. Yesterday, news came of three robbery cases, both on land and water. They are recorded as follows: 1. The Jiangyin Gushan route of the Xinji Steamboat Bureau at Gongyun Bridge. Yesterday (the 17th) morning, around 7:00 AM, it departed from Gushan fully loaded with passengers, heading to Wuxi. When passing the Xili Bridge area, about ten li from Zhangjing Bridge in the seventh district of this county, the steamboat stopped as usual to allow passengers to disembark or board. Unexpectedly, three bandits, carrying two Mauser pistols and a bayonet, disguised themselves as passengers on the steamboat. The purser, Deng, did not suspect anything. When the steamboat reached Huangshan Bridge, the three bandits drew their Mauser pistols, intimidated the passengers, and searched them one by one, losing more than 700 yuan. After the robbery, the bandits cut the tow rope of the tugboat and forced the helmsman to release the steamboat, quickly sailing to Wan'an Bridge, where they abandoned the boat and disembarked, heading towards Dongheng. Afterward, the purser, Deng, called the Xinji Steamboat Bureau to report to the Public Security Bureau and the county government, requesting the dispatch of police to pursue the bandits. After receiving the report, County Chief Chen and Bureau Chief Hua immediately dispatched detectives to the countryside by boat for a thorough pursuit. The police detachment stationed at Zhangjing Bridge and the Huangtutang merchants' association also rushed to hunt them down but were unsuccessful. 2. Cai Shigen and Long A'jun's houses in Shangmadun outside the East Gate were robbed by two thieves on the night of the 16th, one after another, losing more than 100 yuan. 3. Chen Yonggen's house in Yangxiang, near Yanqiao in the fifth district, was also robbed by five or six bandits who broke into the house. Only a silver bracelet was stolen. Chen Yonggen was stabbed in the right arm by the bandits. The case has been reported to the bureau for investigation.

▲ Power Lines Broken, Two Victims: Yesterday morning (the 17th) around 4:00 AM, two power lines, numbers 2253 and 2254, in Xiatang Town outside the South Gate suddenly broke. A vendor from Yancheng, Liu Zhongjing, and Xu A'fu asked the former's eldest daughter, Dabao, to help. After Dabao learned of it, she called a neighbor, Wu Tabao, to go together. Both were electrocuted. Wu died instantly due to the severity of the electric shock. Dabao was rescued with wooden objects and escaped danger. She was immediately sent to the Wuxi Sanatorium for treatment. The bodies of Liu Zhongchen and others were hastily coffined and buried after being examined by the court after a report.

Education News

Important News

Reorganization of Normal Schools 110

▲ The Ministry of Education Held a Meeting to Discuss Yesterday

Nanjing, 17th - The Ministry of Education's ministerial meeting on the 17th discussed the Organic Law of Normal Schools, with changes to the level and duration of normal and rural normal schools: (1) Normal schools and high schools may attach normal classes, recruiting high school graduates for one year of study to serve as elementary school teachers; (1) Normal schools and junior high schools may attach simplified normal classes, recruiting junior high school graduates for one year of study to serve as assistant teachers and simplified elementary school teachers; (1) Simplified normal schools recruit higher elementary school graduates for one year of study to serve as assistant teachers and simplified elementary school teachers.

Anhui Will Not Hold Qualifying Examinations 111

▲ The Department of Education Had Already Issued Orders to Hold Them

▲ Now Suspended Due to Difficulties

The Anhui Department of Education had previously received orders from the Ministry of Education to hold qualifying examinations for primary and secondary school graduates. The department first issued orders to comply, and then formulated detailed measures, deciding to temporarily limit it to provincial middle schools and provincial capital primary schools. This was because the banditry and floods made it temporarily difficult to popularize it throughout the province. Yesterday, the Department of Education again stated that it felt it was also difficult to hold qualifying examinations for provincial middle schools and provincial capital primary schools this semester, and specifically telegraphed the Ministry of Education to request a temporary postponement. The Ministry of Education approved the postponement in a reply telegram. The Anhui provincial graduate qualifying examination will not be held at all this semester.

Mr. Zhu's words made me understand somewhat. However, I still could not deduce what impact the theory of action-producing knowledge would have on our school, so I asked Mr. Zhu to explain it to the end. Mr. Zhu said: "This school of ours is fundamentally different from traditional schools. Traditional schools are like abalone canning companies. Students are like individual cans. Teachers are like canning workers. Pseudo-knowledge is like the stinky fish put in the cans, not cooked, not sterilized, pleasing to the eye but causing nausea and diarrhea and costing one's life if eaten. How can you blame people for throwing away the cans along with the fish! But this canning company is an old shop, bearing the signboard written by the saints and sages of all generations. I won't say anything else, just take Wang Yangming's theory of 'unity of knowledge and action' to discuss it, and you will know that the roots of traditional schools are very deep. He said: 'Knowledge is the beginning of action, and action is the completion of knowledge.' These two sentences represent the educational method of traditional schools. We spend ten or five years in school to do the work of 'knowing' well, and then go outside the school to 'act.' According to the traditional method, if you want to learn to swim, you listen to lectures on swimming in the classroom, read books on swimming in the library, and when it comes to the final exam, you write an essay on swimming and get 70 points to pass, or 100 points to be considered a swimming champion. Who can deny you? Your school has a philosophical basis of knowing before acting, your exam papers have the double circles of PhDs, and your diplomas have the seal of the Ministry of Education. Who can deny you? But you have to be careful, the Dragon King only recognizes skills, not diplomas. If the Da Da steamship catches fire and you are a passenger on board, that will really be a big swimming test. Good, traditional schools must be torn down. Wang Yangming's 'Knowledge is the beginning of action' has to do half a somersault. What is half a somersault? Sun Wukong's somersault is 108,000 miles. He is standing on the palm of Buddha's hand and doing somersaults, and after doing one, he is still standing. Doing one somersault draws 360 degrees, and half a somersault draws 180 degrees, which is exactly upside down. Our theory should be like this:

'Action is the beginning of knowledge, and knowledge is the completion of action.'

We must pursue true knowledge through action. When action encounters difficulties, we cannot help but think. When thought is thorough, we obtain true knowledge. Using true knowledge to act, we embark on the path of creation. Today's school is a place to seek knowledge through action. With the courage to act, we can have the harvest of true knowledge, and the possibility of creation."

National Sports Conference Planned 119

National Physical Education Implementation Plan

▲Inviting Yuan Dunli, Wu Yunrui, and Hao Gengsheng to Compile the Plan丨

(1) Second Preparatory Committee Meeting Held Yesterday

丨Meeting Rules Passed

Nanjing, 17th Telegram: The preparatory committee for the National Sports Conference held its second meeting on the 17th and resolved: (1) To request the Ministry of Education to invite Yuan Dunli, Wu Yunrui, and Hao Gengsheng to form a compilation committee for the National Physical Education Implementation Plan; (2) The period for accommodating members is set from August 15th to August 21st; (3) Several proposals such as the detailed rules of the meeting were passed.

(2) Details of the First Meeting

▲Guo Lianfeng Appointed as Secretary-General

The National Sports Conference, the resolution of the first preparatory committee has been seen in yesterday's telegram, details of the meeting are as follows:

At 3 p.m. on the 16th, the Ministry of Education convened the first preparatory committee for the National Sports Conference. Committee members attending were Chu Minyi, Zhang Zhijiang, Zhou Yawei, Guo Xinshong, Gu Shusen, Li Zheng, Peng Baichuan, Wu Yunrui (represented by Peng Baichuan). Guo Lianfeng attended as an observer. Chu Minyi chaired the meeting, and the following resolutions were made: (1) To revise the organizational outline of the preparatory committee for the National Sports Conference, deleting Article 7 and revising Articles 6 and 8, deleting the words "draft" in the titles (revised draft attached); (2) To revise and pass the draft regulations of the National Sports Conference and submit them to the Minister of Education for approval and implementation; (3) The Ministry of Education will, according to the instructions of the Executive Yuan, consult the Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Transportation to allow members free passage on trains and ships; (4) To send letters to relevant agencies, education departments/bureaus of various provinces and cities, and schools specified in the meeting regulations, requesting them to send representatives to attend on time, and to attach the National Sports Conference regulations; (5) Guo Yunfeng of the Social Education Department of the Ministry of Education was internally appointed as the Secretary-General of the preparatory committee; (6) The conference dates were set for August 16th to August 20th; (7) The preparatory committee is scheduled to hold its second meeting at 4 p.m. on the 17th. The revised and passed organizational outline of the preparatory committee and the National Sports Conference regulations are recorded below.

(3) Organizational Outline of the Preparatory Committee

Article 1: This committee is named the Preparatory Committee for the National Sports Conference of the Ministry of Education, organized by the Ministry of Education.

Article 2: The committee will consist of five to nine members, including the director and section chief in charge of the matter designated by the Minister of Education as ex-officio members, and experts in domestic sports or individuals enthusiastic about promoting sports will be appointed.

Article 3: This committee will handle all preparatory matters for the National Sports Conference, starting from June 1932 and ending on the day the conference concludes.

Article 4: The office of this committee will be located in the Ministry of Education in Nanjing.

Article 5: This committee will have one director who will oversee all preparatory matters, appointed by the Minister of Education from among the committee members.

Article 6: This committee will have one secretary-general, and several staff members for document management and reception, appointed by the Minister of Education from among the ministry's staff.

Article 7: All staff members of this committee are volunteers and will not receive salaries, except for reimbursement of office expenses incurred on official business.

Article 8: This committee may hold committee meetings, convened by the director.

Article 9: This outline will be approved and implemented by the Minister of Education.

(4) Conference Regulations

丨Regulations Defining Membership Qualifications

The National Sports Conference Regulations have been passed by the first preparatory committee, approved by the Ministry of Education, and are ready for implementation. The full text is recorded below:

Article 1: The Ministry of Education, in order to actively promote national physical education, discuss practical issues in sports, formulate national physical education implementation plans, and standardize training policies, will convene the National Sports Conference (hereinafter referred to as "this conference").

Article 2: The members of this conference will be composed of the following personnel: (1) The directors of physical education of various national, provincial, and registered private universities, independent colleges, and the Central Political School; (2) Physical education instructors or directors of public sports venues selected by the education departments/bureaus of various provinces and cities (those directly under the Executive Yuan), one per province/city; (3) Presidents of various provincial, municipal, and registered private physical education colleges; (4) Directors of national and provincial/municipal national martial arts halls; (5) Sports experts selected and hired by the Ministry of Education; (6) One representative each from the Directorate General of Training, the Ministry of Interior, the Ministry of Military Affairs, the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Railways, the Ministry of Transportation, the Central Mass Movement Guidance Committee, the General Headquarters of the Boy Scouts of China, the Central Military Academy, and the Higher Police Academy; (7) Ministers and Vice-Ministers and Directors and Section Chiefs of the various departments of the Ministry of Education.

Article 3: If there is overlap between the experts hired by the Ministry of Education and other representatives, the Ministry of Education may hire others to fill the vacancies.

Article 4: This conference will have one chairperson, to be held by the Minister or Vice-Minister of Education. There will be two vice-chairpersons, one to be held by the chairman of the preparatory committee of this conference, and the other to be elected by the conference.

Article 5: This conference must meet the following two conditions in order to officially convene: (1) More than half of the members in categories 1, 2, and 3 of Article 2 have registered; (2) At least one-third of the members in categories 4, 5, 6, and 7 of Article 2 have registered.

Article 6: This conference will be held in the capital.

Article 7: The conference will be held from August 16th to August 20th, 1932, for a total of five days. If necessary, the Ministry of Education may extend or postpone it as appropriate.

Article 8: The scope of discussion of this conference will be limited to the proposals submitted by the Ministry of Education or by the members in accordance with the procedures stipulated in Article 9.

Article 9: If a member has a proposal, it must be sent to the preparatory committee of this conference two weeks before the meeting for preliminary sorting and inclusion in the agenda. If there is a temporary proposal, it must be co-signed by at least ten members and submitted in writing to the chairman and vice-chairpersons, who will consider including it in the agenda.

Article 10: The resolutions of this conference will be implemented by the Ministry of Education as appropriate. If necessary, the Ministry of Education may submit them to higher-level authorities for approval and implementation, or send letters to relevant agencies for reference.

Article 11: This conference will have several staff members to handle various affairs, details of which will be determined separately.

Article 12: The rules of procedure for this conference will be determined separately by this conference.

Article 13: Experts hired by this conference will be provided with travel expenses at the discretion of the conference, while the expenses for other members will be borne by their respective agencies. However, during the conference, the board and lodging expenses of all members will be provided by this conference.

Article 14: These regulations will be approved and implemented by the Minister of Education.

Article 15: If there are any omissions or inadequacies in these regulations, they will be revised by the Ministry of Education.

World Olympic Games 120

▲Los Angeles Busy with Decorations

▲The Olympic Village is Magnificent

▲Indian Delegation Already in the Village

▲Philippine Team Passed Through Hong Kong to the U.S.

The globally sensational Olympic Games, preparations of all kinds, have been completed. Starting from the 15th, Olympic commemorative tickets were sold. The Los Angeles city authorities are busy decorating the city streets. Just considering the national flags of various countries, the budget is said to be 25,000 yuan. Women's groups use fresh flowers and slogans to decorate the streets, covering every household in the city, thus creating an Olympic atmosphere even in remote alleys.

The competition venues and swimming pools have been completely completed. The Olympic fireworks columns, which will be displayed during the games, reach high into the sky. The record boards for reporting competition results have also been properly arranged. The Olympic Village is considered the most outstanding architectural achievement among the various Olympic buildings. What was once a desolate area of dilapidated houses has now become a magnificent sports village. The main entrance and the general office of the venue are purely Spanish-style buildings. The stands and dining halls around them have been designated for the locations of various countries. It is also said that no visitors are allowed inside during the games, but to facilitate external communication, 70 car permits have been prepared. The Indian team was the first to arrive at this village on the 11th. When the villagers heard the news of the Indian team's arrival, they all went wild with welcome. The Philippine team attending the World Olympic Games arrived in Hong Kong on the 13th aboard the Chichibu Maru. The team leader and coach is Catalon, a group of eight people. Among them, Far Eastern high jump champion Toribio and Far Eastern backstroke champion Yeltai Fangzhou are both expected to score points this time. The team stayed in Hong Kong for one day. The Hong Kong Philippine Sports Association hosted a banquet to welcome them. The team then took the original ship to the United States on the 15th.

Quick Words 126

— Fangzhou

Mr. Huang Qiang, Chief of Staff of the 19th Route Army. He worked diligently in planning strategies and mediating disputes during this war of resistance against Japan and the ceasefire conference. Recently, as the 19th Route Army is about to be transferred to Fujian, he came to Suzhou to preside over everything. President Liao of Suzhou Agricultural School invited him to give a lecture at the school a few days ago. Fortunately, he agreed. Mr. Huang usually doesn't smile easily. On that day, he spoke eloquently for two hours. And his words were witty and humorous, and he emphasized the harm of internal warfare. Those who heard it were moved. Excerpts are below, worthy of the title "quick words."

Mr. Huang recounted his history, saying that he graduated from a French school at the age of sixteen. At the age of eighteen, he served as a translator for the Yunnan-Vietnam Railway Bureau. Because of his anger at the unreasonableness of the French, he abandoned it and went to Guangdong to study the army. Later, he went north and graduated from the Baoding Military Academy. After returning to Guangdong, he served as a lower-ranking officer and participated in the campaign against Yuan Shikai. Later, he fled overseas due to a political change. He studied agriculture and industry in France and aviation in England. After returning to China, he served as the principal of an industrial school and ran a bee farm, chicken farm, and farm, etc. All of them failed due to the impact of internal warfare. However, he never lost heart. Later, he developed Hainan Island, with great plans. He had achieved a lot in twenty months, but his efforts were ruined by a political change. Therefore, he has been engaged in social service for thirty years and has been in the military for twenty years. If calculated according to the example of trade associations, all sectors of agriculture, industry, military, and education can be joined. However, he still has to wear this military uniform and has not been able to find a position in the industrial and agricultural sectors. All because of the impact of internal warfare.

He also said that the result of internal warfare has led to today's poverty and weakness. All taxes are used for military expenses. And in the country, in addition to rampant bandits, the army also disturbs the people wherever it goes. Therefore, bandit areas and places affected by war can be described in a few idioms, namely, "chickens and dogs are not alarmed, nothing is picked up on the road, and doors are not closed at night." Why? Because bandits come like combing and soldiers come like raking. The dogs are all gone, of course, they are not alarmed. Houses are in ruins, nothing can be picked up. There is nothing in the house, so there is no need to close the door. Moreover, military needs are vast, so they must be taken from exorbitant taxes. Therefore, fields are planted with poppies, almost becoming a flower kingdom. For example, villagers who carry goods into the city to sell have a goods tax in the countryside and a landing tax in the city. Passing through the school gate, there is an education tax. Passing through the police station gate, there is a public security tax. Passing through the security group gate, there is a local security tax. Layer upon layer of exploitation finally makes the person abandon the goods and flee. Therefore, Chinese affairs today are not impossible to do. You only need to stop the internal warfare, make the people rich, and then educate them. When I was stationed in Hainan Island, I first spent four months clearing out the communists, then built roads and reclaimed land, and finally checked household registrations and implemented the baojia system. After more than a year, Hainan was well-governed. Every holiday, I went out on horseback alone, stopping a passerby and asking his name, hometown, address, etc., and then checked it against the accompanying register of the township. If what he said was untrue, it would be suspicious. I was able to achieve true "nothing is picked up on the road, and doors are not closed at night." Therefore, government is not about saying more. Being able to recognize the goal and bury yourself in doing it will definitely lead to results. In Hainan Island for twenty months, I never posted a single slogan.

Mr. Huang finally solemnly stated that because he felt the harm of internal warfare, the 19th Route Army will never fire a single bullet internally from now on. Externally, even if there is only one soldier and one soldier left, they will resist to the end.

Crying for Teacher Feng Huifeng 127

— ·Ju· Mo

During the Gengzi and Xinchou years of the Guangxu era, the teacher served as a school official in Lishui County for more than two years. At that time, I was not yet twenty years old. In Bingwu, I came from Hangzhou to Cixi to visit the teacher at his residence. On the Qingming Festival in March of Renshen, I and his family paid respects to the teacher's tomb in the northwest corner of Lake Ci. The grass was already lush. Recalling the past thirty years, it was like a dream. I lowered my head and looked around, not knowing where the tears came from. I got a poem that said: "Events of thirty years ago, all come to mind. I was fifteen or sixteen years old, once swept the jade steps. Wandering in Du Fu's old study, rising to Wu Gong's Terrace. Closing the door to copy poems and articles, not knowing whether I was talented or not. After copying, I took them away, and the teacher knew without a doubt. Sometimes he looked at me and smiled, 'This child's heart is still young.' After leaving, almost ten years passed, studying in Laohuai. (The teacher lived in Cixi Laohuashu Mentou, and there was an old locust tree at the door). From then on, on rainy nights, I often accompanied him in the empty room. If I didn't see him for three days, he would urge me with poems. He often said in sadness, 'My laughter is for you.' I am ashamed of being Yang Gonghe, only accompanying the world in vain. Suddenly thirty years have passed, the child of the past is now old. Last year I was sick, and I heard the teacher dreamt of snakes and vipers. I struggled to cross the sea, and my mind was gray. Before parting, he held my hand, 'How many times can we meet?' I held back my tears, not daring to let them fall, saying that there would be no future disasters. Eleven months after parting, Mount Tai collapsed. Thousands of people cannot redeem it, and a coffin is buried on the mountain's edge. The celestial sphere and jade balance are left to the weeds forever. Today, I worship at the tomb door, and the spiritual wind blows the wine cup. I have already walked away, but I look back, covering my sleeves with lingering sorrow. (Unaccepted reward)"

Touring Chongming in the Rain 128

— Dingming

The Shanghai Yousheng Travel Group has been established for many years. It is divided into small groups such as national music, national art, art, national sound, library, and travel. Among them, the library is a quiet promotion of mass culture, and travel is a dynamic study of natural science. The 12th was the date for the travel group to tour Chongming Island. On this day, the sky was overcast and it rained heavily. However, they still went in the rain. The situation on the day is recorded to mark the footprints.

▲Boat Arrangement: A large ship was rented, which could accommodate more than 500 people. Some did not come because of the rain. Some temporarily joined. There were about 300 people in total. The boat arrangement was quite spectacular. Two large flags with the Yousheng Group emblem were erected on the top of the boat. On the right side of the hull, eleven round lead plates with a diameter of three feet, painted with white characters on a black background, were suspended at parallel intervals. The characters on them read: "Yousheng Travel Group Direct Chartered Boat to Chongming." The boat was three stories high. Everywhere, up and down, left and right, were plastered with the words "[Youth travel helps education], [Adult travel increases experience]," and "[Travel is a method for seeking knowledge, seeking knowledge promotes national evolution]." These are probably the group's motto.

▲Views of the Shanghai-Ying Sea: Mr. Shao Woyun said, "[Chongming Island was formerly known as Yingzhou. The scenery along the way from Shanghai directly to Chongming, passing through the Pujiang River and the sea, is worth seeing everywhere. It is a pity that the ruins of Wusong are broken and unbearable, shocking to the eye. Although the rain is erratic, it is still a feast for the eyes. There are no less than hundreds of warships and ships from various countries on the Pujiang River, connected end to end. In the Yunzao Creek, there are countless sailboats, which are commonly known as the water rickshaws. All of them have triangular red cloths tied high on the masts. Looking back at Pudong, the green fields fill the eyes, adding to the joy of the trip. The wheel crosses the Three Gorges, and suddenly the waves are turbulent, and the sea and sky are vast. It is another natural picture. The wheel docks on Chongming Island. Looking at the wild scenery of Haimen on the opposite bank from afar, the clouds and fog are hazy and vaguely discernible. There are dozens of fishing boats in front, like dragonflies skimming lightly on the water. As it flows back, the wheel gets farther and the island gets smaller. It is also like a golden cicada swimming dragon, lively and knowing people's minds and sending us off. Then the clouds cleared and the sky cleared. Colorful clouds flew for about four hours. Floating into the Pujiang River, to the vicinity of Gaoxing Temple and Jun Gong Road. The sea lights are shining, shining into a mirage. All of this is a rare water town landscape."

Trivial Notes on Health Preservation by an Old Man of Ninety-Three 129

— Jingqing

The noise and dust of Shanghai are very harmful to the years. Therefore, there are not many old people. It is heard that in Kaixian County of Sichuan Province, there is an old man named Li Qingyun, who has reached the age of two hundred and sixty. It is a fact and can be called the giant of longevity in the universe. He has a close relationship with a famous lawyer from Shanghai, Mr. Tan. I was introduced by a friend's letter and was given a photo of the old man. His fingernails are more than a foot long, his forehead is broad and he has no beard, and his eyes are bright. He is indeed a sign of longevity. It is said that this old man is skilled in the ways of Han Kang. At the age of seventy, he climbed mountains. He inadvertently ate some kind of herb and suddenly felt his body stronger than ever. That's how he reached today. It is a pity that I have not been able to get the details. Let's talk about Mr. Xiang's health preservation.

Mr. Xiang has no煩恼 of desires and no disturbance of family. His diet and living habits are all based on scientific rules. He is opposed to the old Chinese health preservation methods and the theories of Zheng Taozhai and others. But he is also different from the health methods of Okuma Shigenobu and Wu Zhirong. Wu and Okuma boasted of living to be a hundred years old, but they only left behind exaggerated words.

Mr. Xiang never eats porridge or rice. He only eats milk, half-cooked chicken eggs (or pigeon eggs), chicken juice, beef juice, and a small amount of bread for three meals a day. He never eats vegetables rich in fiber because they hinder the stomach wall of the elderly and are difficult to digest. For domestic tonics, he only occasionally takes cinnamon oil and white fungus. Although he sometimes drinks ginseng soup, he does not consider it a necessity. He only drinks a small amount of wine with each meal, or takes digestive tablets. He must eat two or three kinds of fruits between lunch and dinner to aid digestion. Among the fruits, he especially likes mangoes, apples, tangerines, pears, etc. He always cuts bananas into the milk and eats them together. He always rinses his mouth and brushes his teeth after meals, and then drinks lemon tea or tea to remove grease. He usually likes to eat (based on physiological theories) honey, green onions, garlic, and wild lilies, etc.

Mr. Xiang once said that there were many long-lived people in ancient Jewish times because they often ate honey, green onions, garlic, etc. In recent years, Western doctors have generally advocated eating green onions, garlic, etc. regularly, which can strengthen the body, especially for those who are weak. Even comparing Northerners and Southerners, most Northerners are stronger, which can be used as evidence. Mr. Xiang also said that Caucasians are mostly over ninety years old because they often eat lactic acid cakes, which can eliminate harmful E. coli and prolong life. As for the Cantonese eating snake meat, he said it is quite in line with science and can treat skin diseases because it has the power to eliminate filth in the body. He highly praised the modern popular meditation method, but he has not practiced it.

Mr. Xiang goes to bed around 9 pm every night. He gets up at dawn, washes and dresses, and goes to the church to recite scriptures and attend Mass, which is his habit. In cold weather, even when the sky is still dark, he must get up early on time, just to go to the church to recite scriptures. In this way, mundane thoughts are washed away, and the heart is at peace. This is also a major reason for enjoying longevity. However, since the rampant Japanese pirates, the pain of national subjugation has often overflowed his words, showing his deep concern for the country.

He often sleeps for one or two hours after lunch to nourish his spirit and aid digestion. He lives on the third floor, where the sunlight and air are good. The building faces green fields, which can relieve eye strain. Looking at the Jiufeng Mountains in the distance, the scenery is pleasant. Leaning on the railing, he enjoys the greenery, and the beauty extends his years. The doors and windows are covered with green gauze to block mosquitoes and flies. He must bathe every day in the hot summer, and even in the cold winter, he must bathe every three days. He rarely exercises, just like Yang Tieya in his later years who did not go downstairs. (A doctor said that if Mr. Xiang could pay attention to exercise after his prime, his physical strength would be stronger.) He sits surrounded by books, never letting go of the books in his hand. He loves learning and is far beyond my reach.

A Glimpse of the Qingdao Aquarium 130

— Jin Junren

The Qingdao Aquarium is built in the middle section of the seaside park. It faces the sea and backs onto the road. The exterior resembles a city wall, magnificent and imposing. Visitors must purchase a ticket for one dime. The center is an open-air courtyard with two fountains that spray water like pearls and jade, which is very interesting. On both sides are display areas for various aquatic species, protected by glass. Inside are stored water, stones, sand, grass, etc., resembling the glass windows of a shop. Each window contains one, two, or three or four types of aquatic animals. Starfish and flounder are rarely seen by people, so they attract the most attention. The shape of a starfish is like a water chestnut, with five corners and gold and white spots on a blue background, which is quite beautiful. However, viewers cannot discern the location of its mouth and eyes, because its shape is round and it is dull and immobile. The flounder is oval in shape, but if we look at it casually, it is only a thin piece of paper, floating up and down, and we cannot see any other body parts. At the end of each aquatic display area on both sides is a large glass room, containing an old dragon, nearly ten feet long. One can imagine that when it lives in the water, it can stir up waves and is fierce and unparalleled. Another room contains specimens of various aquatic species. There are many types of coral, with different names and styles. The establishment of an aquarium in our country is probably the first of its kind. It is said that the cost was quite high. With this construction in the seaside park, the number of visitors will increase even more.

Occasional Notes (82) 131

— Master of Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter 10: Powerful Officials Abuse Authority, Fortunately a Lady Offers Comfort; Expediently Bribing, Achieving Success; Recruiting Bandits and Accepting Surrender

Liang Xiaoyun also stopped these meticulous and affected gestures, and only pulled An Yutian aside to talk about serious matters, saying, "You really don't need to worry anymore. Those people at the Adjutant's Office, don't be fooled by their military officer airs. They all look like human beings, but in reality, they are all extremely lowly errand runners. They just want to find someone to ask for some money. If you have money, you can get them to move. You thought it was right to go through them in a dignified manner to see Old Ye. But since you have to pass through their hands, you have to get them to obediently run errands and deliver your card. This, like the 'door money' movement fee, absolutely cannot be saved. It's better to give it to them straightforwardly and earn some face. Why risk being reckless and barging in, letting them look down on you? The reason I was complaining about you just now was because I didn't want you to be mistreated by them for nothing. Now that things have come to this, you have to get that face back properly. It's inevitable that you'll have to add a little more to the usual amount, and then it'll be over. Tomorrow, I'll have Little Mao come over and tell him to handle it for you. Once it's settled, I guarantee your next visit won't be with that kind of face. Spending a little money has its worth. It's not some kind of unreasonable thing. For example, the male and female servants in our house, who doesn't want to find extra income and earn some pocket money? If we go to other people's mansions for social engagements, we also have to give out some tips. It's just that there's a difference in status and influence. The Adjutant Officer relies on the power of the Military Governor to demand more and be more aggressive. We understand human nature and must follow the customs. We should be more accommodating and generous, so that these subordinates are happy. As the ancients said, 'A small impatience spoils great plans.' Doing great things also requires not being stingy with small expenses." These words made An Yutian admire her greatly, and naturally he no longer cared. The next day, Mao Deshun arrived after receiving a phone call. Liang Xiaoyun completely entrusted him to clear things up and asked him to deliver the gifts. She tore off two bank checks, one for four hundred yuan and one for two hundred yuan, and handed them to Mao Deshun, saying, "This four hundred yuan is solely for Adjutant Wan. Please also ask Adjutant Wan to distribute the two hundred yuan to everyone in the Adjutant's Office as a small token of appreciation. Please ask them to help Councilor An more in the future when he goes to see the Military Governor. When I arrived here, I had already mentioned to Councilor An that we should send them this customary fee. It's just that I've been busy playing mahjong with Fifth Madam these past two days, so I was delayed."

The State of the Financial World After the Settlement 133

After the financial circles of this city concluded the account settlement for the 20th year at the end of last month (May), it was originally expected that they would engage in expanding their business and making efforts to proceed this month, in order to make up for the right to missed business opportunities in the first half of the year. Therefore, in the past two weeks, they have been quite busy with the formalities of distributing account books and establishing accounts. Unfortunately, the overall situation of the entire commercial sector in Shanghai is generally desolate after the disaster, and the economy is exhausted. If they want to develop as much as possible, they are too afraid of the risk. If they intend to choose cautiously, it is indeed an extremely difficult problem for the current shops to raise cash and make up for credit. Therefore, those who want to lend dare not try easily, and those who seek lending have no way to invite people to guarantee their credit. It is still the case that there is a surplus but no adjustment, a deficiency but no filling, and unevenness between fullness and lack, which is probably rarely seen in history. Observing this, the joys and sorrows of commerce this summer and autumn can be witnessed under this situation. Can its depression be described again?

Grain

Rice Market Continues to Drop 20 Copper Coins 143

▲ In the southern part of Shanghai yesterday, about 20 ships from various gangs arrived, and there were more than 200 warehouses in Puxi. Sales in urban and rural shops are difficult to develop due to tight finances. It is also heard that Xinzha is cheaper, and appetites are congested. Thick japonica fresh material has fallen sufficiently. However, the intermediate and late maturing rice has fallen by another 20 copper coins. The demand for early and late rice is very small, and the price has also been reduced. Luxiang indica rice arrivals and sales are both sluggish, and the market continues to be dull.

▲ In the northern part of Shanghai yesterday, Tou Nian No. 3 and 4 from Xinzha Suzhou River arrived. The opening in the morning was limited in its ups and downs. The goods from Xiyi were firmly priced, while the secondary goods were slightly weaker. Although there was not much thin rice, the price remained at the original level. The change in the Yin Yuan market was neither good nor bad. Another round of foreign rice arrived, about 50,000. The customer's appetite was slightly lower, and the local street was dull, causing prices to gradually decline.

Wenzhou Indica Rice Arrives in Large Quantities and Prices Fall 144

▲ Rice stocks are approaching 20,000 bags... Foreign rice sales are sluggish... Continuing to be nearly a corner lower

Yesterday, the foreign rice market was weak in both customer demand and rice arrivals. Rice stocks are full, and there are still many orders. Foreign merchants in the market also have futures for sale. Although no new transactions have been agreed upon, the market and people's hearts have been brought down. The market price of returned goods is also low, and there are no buyers asking about it. Therefore, the spot price continues to be nearly a corner lower. Yesterday, only 200 bags of red large twisted rice were handled by inland offices, priced at 9 yuan and 45 cents. Local and rural offices handled 1,000 bags of small twisted rice, priced at 10 yuan and 02 to 10 yuan and 05 cents. There were no other transactions. The sales of Wenzhou rice have been very good recently, with sales occurring immediately upon arrival. There is no inventory in the market. Recently, merchants have gradually been arriving, and sales have been sluggish. Another batch arrived yesterday, and the city already has close to 20,000 bags in stock. Yesterday, only 340 bags were handled by the local street, and the price fell to over 10 yuan. It is said that the opening price was only 9 yuan and 70 cents.

Flour Market Continues to Decline 145

▲ Actual Sales Have Not Yet Developed

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, the prices for all months uniformly showed a sharp decline. Although the quoted price of foreign wheat did not fluctuate much, the actual sales were unusually weak, and the new wheat was particularly cheap. Although the major factories are still selling spot flour at a loss, the internal and external environment is tending towards stagnation. It seems that the poor economic situation cannot be saved by human power. After the price increase, actual sales could be triggered, then the situation would be transformed. Now, the large-scale sales market has not yet developed. Therefore, it is gradually declining due to natural trends (it is heard that inland manufacturers have dumped goods). The afternoon price for July even broke through the 5-fen mark, and it may return to 80 cents. As a result, the price for July fell by 1 fen and 7.5 li compared to the previous day, the price for August fell by 1 fen and 5 li, the price for September fell by 2 fen, the price for October fell by 2 fen and 2.5 li, and the price for November fell by 2 fen.

Wheat Market Still Weak 146

▲ New Wheat Continues to Arrive, Not Yet Opened

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat futures market in the morning and afternoon, the market prices for all months generally tended to be flat and weak. Although the trend is still not good and the market value of new wheat in the interior is still cheap, local dealers have slightly increased their purchases, and inland gangs are also gradually reducing their positions. Therefore, the supply and demand are evenly matched, and the market atmosphere is relatively stable. However, due to sluggish flour sales, the overall situation is still not good and remains weak. Looking at the next step, if the interior gradually collects cash to hedge, and the factories have no intention of buying, the outcome may still be a small trend. As a result, the price for July was 2 fen lower than the previous day, the price for August was unchanged, the price for September was 2 fen lower, the price for October was 1 fen lower, and the price for November was 2 fen lower. New wheat continues to arrive, but the factories are inactive and have not yet opened for business.

Silk and Tea

Factory Silk Rebound and Sharp Increase 147

▲ European Sales Suddenly Rise, Grade B Price Rises to Over 500 Taels

▲ The Effect of Manufacturers' Persistence, Up 40-50 Taels

Overseas: The sales of white factory silk are sluggish and the price is weak, reaching its extreme point. The price of Grade B has fallen to 420 taels (American market) and 60 taels (French market), with no buyers. The factories all believe that the losses are too great and insist on not selling. Silk sales have been stagnant for a long time. Recently, 100,000 bales of old Japanese silk have been purchased by the Japanese government. After this, raw materials will become scarce. The silk stocks in Lyon are insufficient, and various silk merchants and hoarders have started to buy futures and spot silk. Silk sales in New York are also starting to move, and the market atmosphere has become lively. Chinese merchants' attitude has become more firm. Yesterday, Xinfu Dachang Lianna and other companies imported 140 bales of Grade B top-grade 13-15 filature Shanghai white factory silk spot goods, priced at 520-530 taels, up 40-50 taels. The market is still expected to rise.

Foreign Tea Merchants' Tea Market: Arrivals and Sales are Both Scarce 148

In recent days, the source of Hangzhou green tea has been affected by the mobilization of troops on various routes, and there is a shortage of freight cars between Shanghai and Hangzhou. Cased tea from Anhui and Zhejiang provinces has been accumulated in Hangzhou, reaching a total of 5,000-6,000 cases. The source from the Yangtze River, Qihong tea, has almost run out. Hongcha from Ningzhou in Hubei and Hunan provinces is also scarce. Therefore, only green tea from Wenzhou has arrived in Shanghai in recent days. Tea transactions are also sparse. High-end Qihong tea, Yihua Jinlong and other firms still have sporadic purchases. However, the green tea market is definitely sluggish. Zhenmei and Zhenmei and other items are uniformly trending downwards, and the situation is quite pessimistic.

Sugar Market: Coarse Sugar White Sugar Tends to Fall Again 149

Yesterday, the sugar market's public market trading was still scattered. The price of Dutch No. 24 coarse sugar white sugar fell, with the transaction price at 13 taels and 8 qian, high-quality goods at 13 taels and 9 qian, and Hong Kong goods at 13 taels and 6 qian. Both buying and selling were sluggish, and the market appeared flat. Dutch red No. 8 was at 9 taels and 7 qian, and the trend was still firm. Taikoo refined B Mark was at 16 taels and 1 qian, and CW Mark was at 15 taels and 8 qian and 5 fen. Transactions were also scarce, and the market appeared stable.

Oil Market

White Tung Oil Price Increase Not Yet Over 151

▲ Although Hangzhou is Slightly Weak, the Remote Assistance of Hankou is Strong

Since the source of white tung oil from Hankou has decreased, the situation has turned to rise. Foreign oil companies have also increased prices to 18 taels and 3 qian, which has boosted the market. Dealers' wholesale prices have increased to 15 taels and 2 qian, and then increased by another 3 qian, to 15 taels and 5 qian. Local firms have slightly increased their purchases, but not in large quantities, and the market has become more active. In Hangzhou, due to the scarcity of goods in the production area, the price increased sharply when the Hankou market was weak. However, since the north and south were going in opposite directions, the sales market inevitably declined. Therefore, the highest price was still sold at 29 yuan and 2 jiao per dan. However, the recent Hankou situation has rebounded, and the Hangzhou market has become weaker. According to the details in yesterday's letter, Jinlan and other places sold goods for delivery to Jianggan at 27 yuan and 6 jiao, while the Hangzhou market reported sales to Shanghai at 28 yuan and 4 jiao, which seems to be a slight decrease of several jiao compared to the previous few days. However, since the northern news is good, the strength of the situation in the future is even more predictable.

Local News

Yesterday

Taking Over the Area East of the Songhu Road

All Posts Set up in Districts 5, 1, 2 and 3

Residents Enthusiastically Welcome by Hanging Flags and Setting off Firecrackers

The Japanese army's occupied area north of the Public Concession, east of the Songhu Railway and North Henan Road, falls under the jurisdiction of Districts 5, 1, 2, and 3. Our takeover committee sent personnel to take over at 10:00 AM yesterday. The Japanese naval landing force stationed on Guangdong Street also withdrew towards Jiangwan Road at the same time. The details of yesterday's takeover are recorded below:

▲ Takeover Personnel: The takeover personnel included Huang Ming, Director of the Shanghai North Office of the Public Security Bureau; Gong XiKui, Inspector General of the Public Security Bureau; He Yiming, District Chief of District 5; Ju Jing, Chief of Sub-bureau 1 of District 5; Niu Jingjian, Chief of Sub-bureau 2 of District 5; Wu Tingxun, Chief of Sub-bureau 3 of District 5; Yin Tixin, interpreter; and Nan Qiang, Li Shengjun, Liang Fuchu, Jin Gong, and others from the takeover committee, along with Ma Hongbin, Captain of the Beiping Police Brigade, leading more than 300 Beiping police officers, ready to depart.

▲ Taking Over Defense in Separate Routes: The receiving personnel gathered at the Zhabei Office at about 9:00 AM yesterday. At 9:20 AM, they departed in four batches together with the Police Bureau Chief. The first batch received Sub-bureau 1 of District 5, led by Chief Ju Jing, takeover committee special commissioner Huo Shi, Public Security Bureau translator Bao Ju, a squadron of Beiping police, and a squadron of Shanghai police, totaling 252 people. They took nine cars to the intersection of Qiujiang Road and Songhu Railway, and after contacting Japanese representative Lieutenant Yasuda, they crossed North Sichuan Road to the former site of Sub-bureau 1 of District 5 in eastern Qiujiang Road and got off. After a brief rest, the municipal police took over the areas west of the Shajinggang River. A squadron of Beiping police took over the areas along the border of North Sichuan Road. The second batch received Sub-bureau 2 of District 5, led by Chief Niu Jingjian, and takeover committee special commissioner Li Shengjun, led a second police squad of 84 people to receive the area north of Fusheng Road Qiujiang Road, east of the Songhu Railway, and south of Baoxing Road, and set up posts separately. The third batch received Sub-bureau 3 of District 5, led by Chief Wu Tingxun, takeover committee special commissioner Liu Yumen, and a police squadron of 126 people to defend the area around Hujiamuqiao and Xiangyanqiao. The fourth batch received the General Office of District 5, led by District Chief He Yiming, takeover committee special commissioners Liang Fuchu and Xie Zhidao, and a police squadron of 126 people to receive Dong Yokohama Road and Doulean Road. The Japanese soldiers completed their withdrawal at 10:00 AM, and our side completed the defense and deployment of posts.

▲ Joint Committee Oversight: The takeover committee sent Jin Gong and Cha Nanqiang, together with Huang Ming, Director of the Zhabei Office of the Public Security Bureau, Gong XiKui, Inspector General, and Yin Tixin, secretary, departed at 9:40 AM, first to Sub-bureau 1 of District 5. After receiving reports that the takeover had been completed everywhere, they took six cars to the headquarters of the Japanese naval landing force on Jiangwan Road at about 10:00 AM. At that time, British military officer Bo Mingte, American military officer Bai Longmu, French military officer Peng Naweite, and Italian military officer Fa Tini from the joint committee had also arrived to supervise the exchange between the two sides.

▲ Signing Situation: Our representatives Huang Ming, etc., along with the military officers from the four countries of Britain, the United States, France, and Italy, were received by Japanese representative Captain Onuma Tomio, the commander of the Second Battalion of the Naval Special Landing Force. They gathered at a place to inspect the map and explain the withdrawal of the Japanese army and the defense situation on our side. The Japanese side then presented the handover document, which was divided into three articles. Our side requested the deletion of the compensation issue in the third article, which was a political issue (according to the original text of the article, "[regarding the compensation for losses in the following locations, neither of the two countries shall raise negotiations]"). After Jin Gong and Cha Nanqiang, special commissioners of the takeover committee, and Yin Tixin, secretary of the Public Security Bureau, strongly argued with the Japanese side, Onuma took it to another room, crossed out all the clauses in red pen, and affixed a seal, and then brought it back to show our representatives. Our side was satisfied. Then our representative Huang Ming and Japanese representative Onuma saluted each other. The Japanese representative gave a speech, saying that he was pleased that the Japanese army withdrew and handed over to the Chinese takeover today, and that the order was orderly during the handover, and hoped that the friendship between China and Japan would increase. Our representative Huang Ming replied, saying that after our country took over, we would be obliged to seek order in security and defense to protect the residents. Huang Ming and Onuma signed the handover document at 10:30 AM. Finally, Onuma Tomio and our receiving officers and representatives from neutral countries took a group photo as a memento. It was already 12:00 noon. The military officers of neutral countries left first, and Onuma Tomio and others also shook hands and said goodbye to our receiving personnel one by one.

▲ Japanese Handover Document: The original text of this document is in Japanese, and the translation is as follows: (1) The Japanese army withdraws from the area north of the Public Concession, east of the Songhu Railway and North Henan Road, and west of the Shajinggang River. The Japanese garrison area outside the extraterritorial road construction is not included. (2) The above locations are handed over by the Japanese side to the Chinese side for takeover. Both sides acknowledge and abide by the above items. June 17, Showa 7, Japanese handover commissioner Onuma Tomio, captain of the Third Battalion of the Shanghai Naval Special Landing Force, Chinese takeover commissioner Huang Ming.

▲ Sub-bureau 1 of District 5: At 9:30 AM yesterday, Ju Jing, the chief of Sub-bureau 1 of District 5, led inspectors Gao Hongbin, Wu Baoshu, Li Tingzhang, Huang Yue, and bureau members Guo Chenghai, translator Bao Ju, and 150 Beiping police officers to the bureau to take over. Posts were immediately assigned to 29 locations, including Wusong Road (double posts), Qiujiang Road Xiaocai Market (one post), Qiujiang Road Dongbaoxing Road intersection (one post), Qiujiang Road East Entrance (one post), Qiujiang Road Sichuan Road intersection (double posts), East Qiujiang Road, North Sichuan Road intersection (double posts), Dongbaoxing Road North Sichuan Road intersection (double posts), Xingjiaqiao Road North Sichuan Road intersection (double posts), Xingjiaqiao Road (one post), Gonghe Road (one post), Xinjia Road South Entrance (one post), Dongyang Alley South Entrance (one post), Zejingfang (one post), Huakangli (one post), Jingyili (one post), Qixiufang (one post), Yuqingfang (one post), Third Branch Road Entrance (one post), Changchun Road West Entrance (one post), Aruili (double posts), Shiqingli (one post), Huaxingfang (one post), Daxingli (one post).

▲ Sub-bureau 2 of District 5: At 9:40 AM yesterday, Niu Jingjian, the chief of Sub-bureau 2 of District 5, translator Li Shengjun, staff member Chen Jiwu, and 80 Beiping police officers arrived at Guangdong Street Zhao Qifeng Public Righteous School to meet with Yasuda, the chief of the Japanese Naval Landing Force stationed there. Lieutenant Yasuda set the withdrawal time at 10:00 AM and asked our takeover personnel to wait. Therefore, our side first deployed posts. The 40 or so members of the Japanese Naval Landing Force stationed there withdrew towards Jiangwan Road at 10:00 AM yesterday. Our takeover personnel also moved into Zhao Qifeng Public Righteous School at 10:05 AM. A total of 13 posts were deployed in the area under the jurisdiction of the district, including North Sichuan Road Chuan Highway intersection (one post), Chuan Highway Sanyili (one post), North Sichuan Road Dalideli Entrance (one post), North Sichuan Road Xingjiaqiao Road intersection (one post), Qiujiang Road Zhongshan Road (one post), Zhongshan Road South Entrance (one post), North Sichuan Road Guangdong Street intersection (one post), North Sichuan Road Chongyeli Entrance (one post), North Sichuan Road Qiujiang Road intersection (one post), Xingjiaqiao Road Guangdong Street intersection (one post), Gongjiazhalu North Head (one post), Fusheng Road intersection (one post), Dongxinmin Road (one post).

▲ Sub-bureau 3 of District 5: At 9:30 AM yesterday, Wu Tingxun, the chief of Sub-bureau 3 of District 5, inspectors Zhou Jie and Wang Xuzan, takeover committee special commissioner Liu Yao, security captain Ma Hongbin, and 80 Beiping police officers and 40 Public Security Bureau police officers arrived at the bureau to take over and deploy posts. A total of 15 posts were deployed, including Quanjiapu Road (one post), Pingmin Village (one post), Qimei Road (one post), Yangjiabang (one post), Baoan Road (one post), Xinjia Road (one post), Jixiang Road police station door post (one post), Jixiang Road (one post), Hengfeng Road (one post), Qingji Road (one post), fire brigade entrance (one post), Tiantong Road (one post), Majiali (one post), Tongjia Road (one post), Ruikangli door post (one post).

▲ Residents Rejoice: After our police entered the city, they divided into posts and organized patrol teams to patrol in various parts of the district, once every three hours, divided into two shifts each time, with three policemen in each shift. Therefore, the order was very good, and there was no concern for security. When our police arrived, national flags fluttered along the streets, and residents set off firecrackers to warmly welcome them.

▲ End of the Road for Traitors: When the Japanese army in Shajinggang had not yet withdrawn, traitors gathered there, relying on the power of the Japanese. They opened opium dens and stolen goods dens, including Shunli Company at No. 1 Jishanli, Tiantong Road; Zhonghe Company behind Yue Nai Garden, Disiwei Road; Shunli Branch at No. 1 Lane 44, Shajinggang Road; and Jiufu Company at No. 1 Shandefang, Tiantong Road, and many other places. After our police arrived yesterday, the traitors had already fled upon hearing the news. Only the opium and gambling paraphernalia were seized and brought back to Sub-bureau 3 of District 5. Several servants in the dens were also arrested and taken to the bureau for interrogation.

▲ D-District Issue: As of yesterday, the Japanese army in D-District had not yet withdrawn, numbering about 1,000. Yesterday, Joint Committee Yu Hongjun stated that after the takeover was completed today (17th), the Japanese army in D-District would also be negotiated with the Japanese side within a few days, asking them to withdraw as soon as possible to restore the state before January 28. In addition, there are four locations: Tongwen Academy, Toyota Yarn Factory, Gongda Yarn Factory, and Huafeng Yarn Factory. The Japanese side stated that they could also withdraw from each location, with about 40 or so people, in the next few days.

▲ Takeover Meeting: At 2:00 PM yesterday, the takeover committee held its seventh committee meeting at the United Nations Building. The attendees were four committee members: Yin Rugeng, Guo Dehua, Wen Yinxing, and Zhu Xibai. Han Deqin was absent from Shanghai due to business. Routine matters were discussed, and the meeting adjourned at about 3:00 PM.

Wang Jingwei Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 152

Returns to Nanjing by Train the Same Evening

▲ Meets with Song Chen to Make a Final Entreaty

▲ Also Explains the Results of the Lushan Conference

▲ Song Ziwen May Go to Nanjing Soon

President of the Executive Yuan Wang Jingwei, accompanied by Central Committee member Li Shizeng and his wife Ms. Chen Bijun, arrived in Shanghai by plane from Nanjing at 4:00 PM yesterday. Mr. and Mrs. Wang returned to their residence to rest. At 5:00 PM, Wang went to the Chen residence on Shan Zhong Road to visit Chen Mingshu, detailing the Lushan Conference and firmly urging Chen to resume his duties as soon as possible. Chen declined on the grounds of poor health and the need for temporary recuperation, and there was still no concrete result. After talking for about half an hour, Wang bid farewell. At 8:00 PM last night, Wang went to the Song residence on Qi Qi Road to visit Song Ziwen. In addition to explaining the overall central financial plan decided at the Lushan Conference, he also sought Song's opinion. At that time, Song expressed no objection. Wang then urged Song to go to Nanjing as soon as possible to cancel his leave and resume his duties. Wang left the Song residence at about 9:00 PM. The purpose of this trip to Shanghai was to meet with Mr. Song and Mr. Chen to explain the new plan for military, diplomatic, and financial affairs and to make a final entreaty. At the same time, because government affairs in Nanjing were complicated, he had no time to stay longer. He hurriedly took a special train from Fanhuangdu Station back to Nanjing at 10:20 PM last night. It is said that Song Ziwen has agreed to cancel his resignation after Wang's repeated and earnest request, and he is expected to go to Nanjing to resume his duties in the near future. As for the rumors that the national government will be reorganized and Sun Ke will be appointed as the President of the Executive Yuan, they are mostly speculative.

Gu Weijun 153

Flew to Beijing this morning

▲ Yesterday afternoon, banking circles held a banquet to honor him.

▲ In the evening, St. John's University classmates held a welcome dinner.

Mr. Gu Weijun, the Chinese representative of the League of Nations Investigation Team, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing. People from all walks of life, in recognition of Mr. Gu's resolute and arduous journey, have successively held events to express their appreciation. Mr. Gu was originally scheduled to leave Shanghai yesterday, but due to the overwhelming kindness of various sectors, he stayed for one more day and decided to take a flight to Beijing this morning to meet with the Investigation Team. The following is a record of Mr. Gu's activities yesterday:

▲ Responded to a banquet by banking circles. Mr. Gu received relatives and friends at home yesterday morning. At 1:15 PM, accompanied by Zhang Xianglin and others, he attended a luncheon hosted by the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and leading figures in the banking industry at the Bankers' Club. Those present included Xu Jilou, Qian Xinzhi, Lin Kanghou, Xu Xinliu, Guo Bingwen, Shi Liangcai, and others. Mr. Gu, along with Zhang Xianglin and other guests, totaled about thirty or forty people. During the meal, Qian Xinzhi stood up to deliver a congratulatory speech on behalf of the banking community, followed by Mr. Gu who also gave a speech in response. During the banquet, Mr. Gu provided detailed reports on Northeast China's financial situation. The banquet concluded at 2:30 PM with the guests and hosts parting on amicable terms.

▲ The Alumni Association of St. John's University hosted a dinner. Mr. Gu is an alumnus of St. John's University, and the Alumni Association held a banquet last night at 8:00 PM in the Continental Emporium building to welcome him and express their appreciation. Mr. Gu arrived to a round of applause from all the alumni, shaking hands and exchanging greetings with each classmate. They chatted freely during the meal. Everyone dispersed around 11:00 PM.

▲ Flew to Beijing this morning. Mr. Gu, considering that the Investigation Team is scheduled to depart for Japan within days and that his duties are not yet completed, decided to return to Beijing this morning. At 8:30 AM, he took the original flight from Hongqiao Airport to Beijing. After arriving in Beijing, he plans to pay respects to Premier Wang and Minister Luo. In the afternoon, he will fly north from Beijing and is expected to arrive in Beiping around 5:00 PM.

▲ Decided to accompany the delegation to Japan. During his previous trip outside the customs, Mr. Gu was subjected to threats from rebels in the Northeast. Despite various obstacles upon arriving in the Northeast, he continued to advance with a resolute determination. His spirit and perseverance are truly admirable. As the Investigation Team drafts its report, they decided to begin in Tokyo, Japan, and complete it in Beiping. Mr. Gu, after being urged by key figures such as Chiang and Wang in both Nanjing and Lushan, agreed to accompany the delegation to Japan and has decided to depart for Japan when the Investigation Team leaves Beiping.

▲ Mr. Gu firmly stated that yesterday's news reported a Reuters dispatch from Tokyo on the 16th, which contained threats against Mr. Gu. A reporter from the Central News Agency specially visited Mr. Gu yesterday to inquire about his opinion. According to Mr. Gu's statement to the reporter, he has not yet seen the dispatch. However, this is an issue for the Investigation Team and is unrelated to him personally. As for his acceptance of the government's order to accompany the Investigation Team to Japan, he will maintain his past spirit, not shy away from difficulties, and resolutely accompany the Investigation Team on their trip to Japan. He will fly to Beijing tomorrow morning to meet with Foreign Minister Luo before heading north, as Minister Luo still needs to hold a meeting with the members of the Investigation Team.

▲ Representatives of the National Salvation Association visited. The Shanghai United Association of National Salvation Groups previously held a regular meeting at its premises on Guling Road and appointed Yin Zhiling and Tan Bozhi to visit Mr. Gu to express their appreciation and inquire about diplomatic policies. Mr. Gu personally invited them for a detailed discussion at his residence last night about the diplomatic policies that should be adopted in the future. The association appointed Yin Zhiling, Chu Huiseng, and Li Cishan to visit as agreed and discuss future diplomatic policies with Mr. Gu for about an hour. All possible diplomatic approaches were discussed in detail.

Furthermore, the association received a letter yesterday from the Chaozhou Shanghai Fellow Association, stating in brief that the Northeast has fallen for nine months, the government has made empty promises of resistance and watched idly as it was devastated. The Northeastern Volunteer Army could not bear to see their compatriots subjected to the enemy's cruelty and could only resist with flesh and blood, pressing forward one after another, regarding death as returning home. Reports say that Representative Gu Weijun said during his return to Beiping that the people outside the customs only ask when the government will recover the Northeast. How tragic this statement is! If one has no heart, how can one bear to not save them? Since the people in all parts of our country cannot share the dangers of fire and water with the Northeastern Volunteer Army, if they do not provide economic assistance, how much different would that be from watching without saving? Moreover, given the ambitions of the Japanese bandits, if the Northeast is lost, other provinces will inevitably be threatened. If we treat them like the people of Qin treated the people of Yue, we will all perish in the end. Your association spares no effort to promote donations, running around and appealing, which is deeply admirable. Our association has now raised 1,000 yuan in silver dollars from anonymous donors and is sending it along with this letter. Please remit it to the Northeast immediately to provide relief. Although it is a drop in the bucket, it serves as a whole fur coat to protect one armpit. Although the Northeast is only a corner, it cannot resist the violent Japanese invaders throughout the country. However, if the national lifeline can be extended, wouldn't the 400 million Chinese people have heroes rise up to lead the people to recover the lost land? As long as there is a breath of life left, we can only do our best and continue to raise more funds for future shipments. All 1,000 yuan of donations have been directly delivered to the Bank of China, and an official receipt has been obtained. Recently, the amount of donations from all sectors for the Northeastern Volunteer Army has surged. The Relief Association is now following the procedures stipulated in its regulations to petition the Custody Committee to immediately remit the funds to the Northeast to provide relief to the Volunteer Army.
