Problem of Reducing or Waiving Rent 157

▲ The municipal government consulted yesterday

▲ Meeting again on the 25th

The Shanghai Municipal Government convened a discussion meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday, gathering representatives from both landlords and tenants involved in the rent reduction and waiver movement to seek solutions. Those present included Yu Hongjun from the Shanghai Municipal Government, Sun Yongyi from the Social Affairs Bureau, landlord representatives Pan Xulun, Wu Baodi from the Nanshi landlords, Shen Lianfang from the Zhabei landlords, representatives of the Rent Reduction and Waiver Movement Committee Yu Hualong, Zhang Henghai, Zhang Yichen, Wang Hanliang, Li Yongxiang, and Zhang Xiaolin and Gui Yanfang from the Shanghai Local Association, Luo Qinghua from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, etc. The meeting was chaired by Yu Hongjun, who first delivered an opening speech, followed by Pan

Page 14

Xulun explaining that the owners also sympathize with the reduction or waiver of rent, but according to the General Principles of Civil Law, rent waivers are permissible when the premises are not occupied, but requests for rent waivers for occupied premises are inappropriate, and so on. Subsequently, Yu Hualong, Gui Yanfang, Shen Lianfang, and others spoke one after another to debate. Yu Hongjun then spoke, stating that he was pleased that the meeting had reached a consensus on the principle of rent waiver. Finally, it was decided to submit the seven measures proposed by the Rent Reduction and Waiver Association to the landlord representatives to formulate their opinions and submit a written statement to the municipal government for review. It was also decided to convene another meeting of both parties on the 25th of this month (Saturday). The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM.

The seven rent reduction and waiver measures proposed by the tenant representatives in Shanghai's district are appended below: (1) Rent for February, March, and April of this year in the areas north of the Suzhou River and in Hongkou and Yangshupu shall be waived entirely. Starting in May, further decisions will be made depending on the local situation. (2) Rent for February and March of this year in Nanshi, Pudong, and the extraterritorial road areas in western Shanghai shall be waived entirely. Starting in April, rent shall be paid at 40% of the original rent until the local situation returns to normal. (3) Rent for February and March of this year in the entire area south of the Suzhou River and in the French Concession shall be waived entirely. Starting in April, rent shall be paid at 50% of the original rent until the situation returns to normal. (4) Rent shall be waived entirely in the areas of Zhabei, Jiangwan, Wusong, Zhenru, and other areas, as well as areas north of the Iron Gate in the Public Concession or adjacent areas, until the situation returns to normal. (5) Except in districts (1) and (4), tenants shall pay for public electricity and tap water during the rent waiver period, and sub-landlords may collect these fees from sub-tenants on a pro rata basis. (6) Tenants in all districts shall enjoy the same rent reduction and waiver rights during the reduction period. (7) During the rent reduction and waiver period, neither landlords against tenants nor sub-landlords against sub-tenants may use excuses to force eviction or increase rent.

A Glimpse into Foreigners' Psychology 158

▲ Disapprove of Establishing a Free City

▲ But Advocate Not Stationing Troops, Chinese or Foreign

▲ In short, it harms Chinese sovereignty

The Mainland News reported that yesterday, an official from the Public Works Department told the Mainland News reporter that the rumored Shanghai Free City plan is an unfeasible plan, directly violating the Nine-Power Treaty, and the Chinese government will ultimately not agree. If the great powers force China to implement it, it will infringe upon Chinese sovereignty. Therefore, although there has long been talk of a free city plan, it initially originated in 1862, and all countries have consistently rejected it. Even if the embers are rekindled this time, they will still be rejected by the great powers. He believes that a better plan that is easier to implement is to designate the area around Shanghai as a non-military zone, with a radius of approximately 20 or 30 miles from Shanghai, where neither Chinese nor foreign troops may be stationed. He believes that all countries concerned would benefit from this plan. Just as the Japanese army used the Public Concession as a base to attack the Chinese army, if the British and Americans wanted to use force to prevent the Japanese from taking this action, they would inevitably have to go to war with Japan. If Shanghai and its vicinity become a non-military zone, the Concession can be guaranteed as a neutral zone, and the recent hostilities would not have occurred. He believes that if the relevant powers sign a treaty with China to make Shanghai a neutral zone, many outstanding issues could be resolved. The reporter asked what the great powers would do if Japan or another country were to violate the neutrality. The official replied that the signatory countries could take joint action to force that country to respect Shanghai's neutrality. In short, Shanghai cannot be transformed into a free city without China's full consent, and he does not believe that China can agree to this. (Translator's Note: Although it is not explicitly stated, whether this official's words can represent the Public Works Department, it can indeed be said to represent the views of most important foreigners in Shanghai. But think about it, what impact would it have on China's sovereignty if Shanghai were to become a treaty-agreed non-military neutral zone? Would it not become a situation of "sacrificing to the gods, I am only nominally the master, but practically dead"? If I have a house and the neighbors agree, "You don't need to send people to guard this house, we neighbors will jointly guarantee its neutrality," then who would practically own this house? No need for wise men to debate it. If Shanghai were to become an agreed-upon non-military zone, wouldn't it be similar to this house? Then the Westerner's proposal is only one step away from a free city. Among the residents of Shanghai, there may be those who are concerned with their own interests, blinded by short-term gains, and secretly sympathize with the no-stationing-troops proposal. If they use the analogy of a house and give it some thought, they will surely realize that it is impossible.)

Post-War Reconstruction Funds for the Shanghai-Songhu Battle Zone 159

▲ The funds were borrowed from the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Central Bank for 300,000 yuan

▲ 150,000 yuan has already been allocated to both the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Jiangsu Provincial Government.

Regarding the post-war reconstruction and relief efforts in the Shanghai-Songhu Battle Zone, the central government has organized the Shanghai-Songhu Battle Zone Reconstruction Committee to take charge of everything. A reporter from the China Eastern News Agency visited Mr. Zhang Shouyong, a standing committee member of the committee, yesterday to inquire about the recent progress of the committee. According to Mr. Zhang, the relief funds were decided to be 1.1 million yuan at the second meeting. The method of bearing the funds has now been decided: the central government will bear 500,000 yuan, the local associations in the city will bear 300,000 yuan, the Shanghai Municipal Government will bear 150,000 yuan, and the Jiangsu Provincial Government will bear 150,000 yuan. Currently, the committee believes that relief efforts are urgent and cannot be delayed, so it has requested the central government to allocate relief funds as soon as possible. The central government then ordered the Ministry of Finance to negotiate with the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Central Bank for the first batch of loans of 300,000 yuan. This loan has no guarantees or interest, and the Ministry of Finance will repay 100,000 yuan from the national treasury each month. The three banks have now handed over the funds to the committee, which has decided on a distribution method: 150,000 yuan to the Shanghai Municipal Government and 150,000 yuan to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, to handle relief efforts separately. The scope of relief currently starts with emergency relief, such as assisting the reconstruction of the battle zone for the masses, providing economic relief to small businesses, and compensating farmers' planting, etc., all of which are handled by the respective provincial and municipal governments. In addition, 20,000 yuan has been advanced by the committee for epidemic prevention, which will be handled by the epidemic prevention team. The remaining 800,000 yuan of relief funds can be collected at any time, so that they can actively engage in disaster relief work. However, 1.1 million yuan is really a drop in the bucket for the battle zone, so the committee must continue to find ways to raise funds.

The Chamber has compiled a register and submitted it to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau for record.

▲ Assembly Agenda (1) Play music to open the meeting; (2) All stand at attention; (3) Bow three times to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of the Premier; (4) The Chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will; (5) The Chairman delivers an opening speech; (6) Speech from the superior authorities; (7) Signing the term of office for the executive and supervisory committee members; (8) Discussing motions; (9) Electing executive and supervisory committee members: A. Counting the number of representatives present; B. Appointing scrutineers; C. Appointing tellers; D. Distributing ballots; E. Voting; F. Opening the ballot box; (10) Reporting the names of the elected executive and supervisory committee members; (11) The Chairman delivers a closing speech; (12) Play music to adjourn the meeting.

▲ Rules of Procedure (1) Please stand when speaking; (2) Please report your seat number before speaking; (3) Do not speak at the same time as another person; (4) Please do not speak more than three times on one motion; (5) Each speech should not exceed five minutes. If it is necessary to extend the time, please request permission from the chairman first; (6) Please be concise and clear when speaking; (7) Please do not applaud others when they are speaking; (8) Please do not speak after the chairman declares the discussion of a motion concluded; (9) Please do not talk during the meeting to avoid interfering with hearing; (10) If you need to leave early, please request permission from the chairman first. ▲ Re-electing Executive and Supervisory Committee Members The Chamber's articles of association stipulate that there shall be 15 executive committee members and 7 supervisory committee members, with a term of four years, with half of the members re-elected every two years and not allowed to be re-elected. The term of office for the first committee members shall be determined by drawing lots. This session is the Chamber's first re-election of committee members. Seven executive committee members and three supervisory committee members who have completed their terms should be selected by drawing lots. The executive committee has decided that those who are drawn shall be considered to have completed their terms, and those who remain shall be considered to have been re-elected, and has submitted this to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for approval. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, as the competent authority, should execute the drawing of lots, and the Chamber has prepared the lottery drum and all the lots in order to hold the event today.

▲ Important Motions There are many important motions for the Chamber's General Assembly, such as (1) the executive committee proposes to issue a declaration, expressing that this year's work should focus on abolishing civil war and promoting domestic goods; (2) the executive committee proposes a motion on war zone debt; (3) the executive committee proposes a motion on establishing a national crisis savings fund; (4) Ma Shaoquan and Luo Qinghua propose a motion to issue a declaration opposing the Shanghai Free City; (5) Wang Yansong, Lu Fengzhu, and others propose to petition the government to demand that Japan compensate for the losses of the Shanghai War; (6) Wang Yansong and Zheng Chengqing propose to petition the central government to issue a circular to party and government agencies in various places to earnestly eliminate labor-capital disputes, increase domestic production, and cultivate national strength to save the country from disaster; and budget resolutions and more than 20 important motions from various labor unions.

Be Careful of Munitions in the Battle Zone 161

▲ Report to the police on duty immediately if discovered

▲ Carefully excavate and remove them

Shanghai Public Security Bureau Proclamation Zheng No. 17: Proclamation regarding the discovery that since the Shanghai Incident occurred, there are munitions left behind in all battle zones. Civilians who accidentally touch them may die or be disabled. The director of this bureau has repeatedly received reports from various districts that there have been multiple cases of accidental contact resulting in death or injury, which is very sad. Therefore, we sincerely proclaim that all citizens should inform their sons and brothers that from now on, whenever and wherever dangerous goods are discovered, they should immediately report them to the police on duty, who will forward the report to the various districts for careful excavation and removal. Do not lightly pick them up, carry them, or throw them away arbitrarily, so as not to cause great misfortune and regret. This proclamation is important. June 18, 21st year of the Republic of China, Director Wen Yingxing.

April's 162

Japanese Imports Increased Sharply

According to a report by the China International Trade Association, the value of foreign goods imported in April was 110,313,287 customs taels, and the value of exported goods was only 49,682,988 customs taels, resulting in a trade deficit of 60,630,299 taels. In January and February of this year, Japanese imports were less than 9 million taels. In March, they increased to more than 13 million taels. In April, they increased again to more than 20 million taels. From January to April, Japanese imports accounted for more than 13%, still occupying an important position among imported goods. In addition, the total value of imports from January to April this year was 370,571,964 customs taels, and the total value of exports was 190,819,873 customs taels, resulting in a total trade deficit of 179,752,091 taels. It was found that Japanese imports decreased during the Shanghai Incident in January and February, but they are expected to gradually increase in the future, and the total value of imports in the 21st year of the Republic of China will inevitably present an unprecedented record.

Changes in Haizhou Port 163

▲ Abandoning Dapu and rushing to build Xugou

Haizhou is the focal point of the Longhai Railway. In recent years, since the opening of the Haizhou liner service in Shanghai, goods from the Northwest that used to be transported to the Southeast via Hankou, Xuzhou, and Nanjing are now transported via Haizhou. Dapu is the main port for transportation in Haizhou. However, the port has been changing, and Dapu's draft has recently become unusually shallow, and merchant ships often encounter accidents, which hinders the transportation of goods. In order to develop its business and facilitate transportation, the Railway Bureau has opened a new port in the northeast. Both the station and the wharf will be built and ready in two months. The details of this matter are investigated and reported as follows:

▲ Flourishing Shipping in Haizhou Since the opening of the port in Haizhou, goods on the Longhai Railway can be transshipped to Shanghai through that port. Dapu is the point of contact for the carriages. There are two shipping companies in Shanghai that have special joint transportation agreements with the Longhai Railway, China Merchants and Dazhen, which jointly dispatch the Tonghua, Yongping, and Yong'an liners. The Hezhong Company also dispatches the Xuzhou and Zhengzhou liners to travel between Shanghai and Haizhou. This route was also suspended during the Shanghai War, but it has now returned to normal. The main imports are miscellaneous grains, oil soybeans, and water tobacco, and the main exports are foreign groceries, sugar, cloth, and paper cigarettes.

▲ Difficult Navigation in Dapu Dapu is Haizhou's only port. Shanghai is about 410 nautical miles away. The Longhai Railway has specially built a railway to transport goods, and the wharves for each liner are also located in that port to facilitate loading and unloading. However, the water level fluctuates. During the shallowest part of the summer, it is only four or five feet, so merchant ships often run aground and accidents occur. Even during high tide, it is only possible to load 500 or 600 tons of cargo, and it is difficult to travel with more. Therefore, the shipping industry feels deeply inconvenienced.

▲ Building a New Port in Xugou The Longhai Railway Bureau, realizing that Dapu cannot develop its business, decided to open a new port to facilitate transportation. After surveying and verification, there is a bay leading to the sea about 45 nautical miles northeast of Dapu. The place name is Xugou, and the draft is very deep, making it most suitable for sea liners to stop. Vessels weighing four or five thousand tons can also enter and exit freely. In the past, the Railway Bureau had the intention of opening Xugou as a commercial port and invited German engineers to estimate that it would cost 20 million yuan to build the port, so the matter was stopped. Now, it has decided to build a railway in Xugou, add warehouses, and deepen the seaport for liners to anchor. Various projects are being rushed to completion.

▲ Can Be Realized in Autumn After the new port in Xugou is built, the Railway Bureau will dismantle the railway in Dapu. The liner wharves will also be moved to the new port, and the port of Dapu will be completely abandoned. The station, tracks, and warehouses will be completed soon, and the Ministry of Finance is also building a customs house there to collect customs duties on imports and exports. It is expected that the entire project will be completed in August of this year. However, due to the fact that the seawall has not yet been built at the liner wharf, it will only be possible to anchor on the surface of the port at that time, and cargo will be loaded and unloaded by barges. After February, the new port in Haizhou can be realized and completed.

Various Sectors 166

Oppose the Opium Monopoly

▲ Anti-Narcotics Association The Chinese National Anti-Narcotics Association held a meeting of its Standing Committee yesterday at the Navy YMCA on Sichuan Road. Attendees included Wang Jingqi, Li Denghui, Ding Shujing, Cai Rudong, Shen Gao, Chen Lingyun, Huang Jiawei, Wu Xiaofen, and others. The meeting proceeded as scheduled. First, Huang Jiawei reported on the association's affairs and the opposition to the opium monopoly over the past month. Then, the meeting discussed plans for future activities: (1) It was resolved to continue to oppose the government's rumored plan to implement an opium monopoly to the end. It was also proposed that, given the government's economic difficulties, alternative tax revenue measures should be proposed to offset the income from the monopoly. Based on a suggestion from Committee Member Li Denghui, this proposal would be submitted to each executive committee member to solicit opinions before being presented to the government. (2) The 22 articles of anti-smoking advocacy drafted by the association's secretariat were approved, and the association would seek input from other anti-narcotics organizations before submitting them to the government. (3) The National Anti-Narcotics Representatives Conference was decided to be held on August 29, the anniversary of the Treaty of Nanjing, in Hangzhou. All national anti-narcotics organizations would be notified to send representatives to participate. All preparatory matters would be handled by the secretariat in conjunction with the Zhejiang Provincial Anti-Narcotics Association. (4) It was resolved that the association's monthly publication, the "Anti-Narcotics Monthly," would be expanded in scope and refreshed in content starting with the July issue (No. 56), transforming it into a general magazine. A contest would be held to solicit a new name. The meeting adjourned after these discussions.

▲ Academic Circles The Shanghai University Students' National Salvation Association, in protest against the opium monopoly, sent a letter to the Central Anti-Smoking Committee, clearly stating their anti-smoking stance. The original letter is recorded below: "To the esteemed Central Anti-Smoking Committee: Since the implementation of the opium monopoly during the seventh year of the Republic, public resentment has been boiling, and we are shamed before the world. Laws are disregarded, and public opinion is rising. The National Government, examining the advantages and disadvantages and heeding public sentiment, established your esteemed committee. At that time, a national anti-smoking conference was convened, and an anti-smoking plan was formulated. The opium demon was terrified, and local dealers were chilled. This was indeed a glorious moment. We believed that from then on, China's anti-smoking efforts would move from darkness to light. All yearned for this, and the entire population shared the same hope. However, in the three years since, we have not heard of any significant achievements. The rampant opium scourge in various regions remains the same as before, or even worse. In recent years, the government appointed Li, who has long promoted the evil theory of opium monopoly, and Wu Liande, known as the "Opium Monopoly Doctor," as anti-smoking commissioners, without stern rejection. Fragrant and foul are placed in the same container, and black and white are indistinguishable, leading to the withdrawal of righteous individuals and attracting the covetous eyes of those who profit from poison, who are constantly thinking about the opium monopoly. The management of narcotics and anesthesia has already deviated significantly from the original intention. What is the point of the state setting up this superfluous agency? Why should the people have one more enemy in the form of a monopoly? It is observed that twelve provinces, including Ji and Sui, have successively implemented disguised monopolies. Your esteemed committee, as the central anti-smoking headquarters, has not issued any punishments. Instead, you have lobbied for support, deliberately imitating the provinces to compete for profits. The central government has lost its dignity and its legal authority. The blame still lies with the central government. We recall that when Zhejiang Province was about to implement a monopoly, the provincial government resigned en masse in protest, and the plan did not proceed. This year, Fujian Province is implementing a monopoly, and the entire provincial committee has requested to be dismissed. Although the goal of banning opium has not been achieved, they can at least hope to be blameless. If names are not correct, words are not smooth; if words are not smooth, things cannot be accomplished. The repeated failures of the opium monopoly are due to this. If your esteemed committee still has sincere intentions to ban opium, please quickly rectify your hearts, abandon the fantasies of recent years, and strive to start anew with the people. When the central authorities are wavering on the issue of opium prohibition, a word of correction from your esteemed committee may bring some stability. If you wish to express your intentions, the precedents of Zhejiang and Fujian may be followed. Otherwise, as we have already said, why should the people have one more enemy in the form of a monopoly? Public opinion will impose its own sanctions. At this critical juncture, we urge all of you in your esteemed committee to reflect on yourselves, make a decisive choice, and lead the new capital. We will quietly observe the results. Written in haste, we have not fully expressed our thoughts. Respectfully addressed to the Central Anti-Smoking Committee. Sincerely, Shanghai University Students' National Salvation Association."

▲ Business Circles The Shanghai Niuzhuang, Zhifu, and Xiamen Three-Route Business Federation yesterday sent a telegram opposing the opium monopoly. The telegram reads: "To the Chinese National Anti-Narcotics Association and all national organizations: The tide of the opium monopoly has been surging for a long time. Recently, the government has decided to try a final measure and implement a monopoly, engaging in a life-and-death battle with the people. The news has arrived, and we want to cry but have no tears. The harm of the opium monopoly is known to everyone. Now the government is abandoning the path of light and choosing the path of certain death. It is evident that the country and the nation will be completely lost, and the tragedy of destruction is imminent. We earnestly request that your esteemed association strive to fight, adhere to a thorough and uncompromising spirit, and fight the evil forces to the end. Our federation is willing to lead all merchants and citizens as a rearguard. Shanghai Niuzhuang, Zhifu, and Xiamen Three-Route Business Federation kowtow. (Signed)"

Both Sides Still Insist Yesterday

▲ Emergency Meeting Held, Three Declarations Issued

▲ Strike Committee and Foremen United

The labor strike at the Concession Telephone Company has become serious since negotiations broke down. The police have taken special precautions. The strike committee held an emergency meeting to decide on next steps and consulted with foremen on ways to unite. The details are as follows:

▲ Management's Hard Line Yesterday, the main office on Jiangxi Road and all branches and warehouses were heavily guarded by the police for protection. The company's attitude remained tough, insisting on unconditional resumption of work. Furthermore, the foreman Tang Liangzhi, Sun Guang, and others negotiated with the company privately and clashed with the strike committee, which significantly affected the future of the strike. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, the strike committee, at the request of the workers, consulted with the foremen at the Far East Hotel on ways to unite. It is reported that all parties reached a mutual understanding and will unite from today onwards to prepare for the outside world.

Recent News on the Extra-Settlement Roads Case 169

▲ The Public Works Department Did Not Discuss It

The Continental Daily reports that, according to a statement by Feixin Dun, Director-General of the Public Works Department, the issue of extra-settlement roads was not discussed at the Public Works Department's board meeting on Wednesday. There is currently no change to the issue. It is reported that the Public Works Department and the Shanghai Municipal Government's Special Committee had previously discussed the matter and reached a settlement agreement, stipulating that the roads would be governed by the Shanghai Municipal Government, and the Public Security Bureau would send police to guard them, but foreign supervisors would be hired. This agreement has not yet been formally submitted to Consul-General Cunningham. It is said that it will be submitted after the Public Works Department and the Shanghai Municipal Government approve it. After submission, it will be submitted to the Consular Body, the Diplomatic Corps, and the National Government for approval. Currently, the concession police and the Public Security Bureau police are providing services as usual on the extra-settlement roads. The concession police patrol the North Sichuan Road area, while the Chinese police stand guard at the entrances to the side streets leading to North Sichuan Road. Since the Chinese police took up their posts, most of the Chinese shops from Bazilu, North Sichuan Road to a certain point outside Shigaota Road have reopened, but they close early. At night, there are hardly any pedestrians on the streets outside Qiujiang Road.

Local News Two

Murder Case of an American Woman 170

▲ Chatting and Laughing in the Car, Shooting Down Below

▲ Abandoning the Body in a Creek, Leaving Calmly

▲ The Driver Was Terrified

▲ The Murderer is the Tianjin Bank Manager

Near Lincoln Road and Warren Road in western Shanghai, a Western assassination case occurred at around 11 AM yesterday. Both the victim and the assailant were Americans. Under the pretext of hiring a car, they went together westward. When they reached the intersection of Lincoln Road, the assailant ordered the driver to stop the engine. Then he and the victim got out of the car one after another, pretending to talk. The assailant pulled out a pistol from his pocket and fired two shots at the victim. One shot hit the victim's right waist, and the other hit the victim's head. Both shots hit vital points, causing instant death. Afterwards, the body was carried back to the car, and the driver was ordered to continue driving. After about three minutes, the body was thrown into the creek there. The murderer then fled north without a trace. The circumstances are bizarre. The details are as follows:

▲ Two Westerners Hire a Truck At around 11:10 AM yesterday morning, two well-dressed Westerners suddenly came to the United Automobile Company on Rue Mère Marie-Thérèse in the French Concession, claiming that they wanted to rent a truck to transport boxes and luggage to the Avenue Haig. At that time, the company did not have a truck, but for the sake of good service, they used the telephone to borrow a truck from the nearby Tanle Company for trial use. The number was noted as 56, and it was driven by Zhao Zhiliang, a Ningbo driver.

▲ Shooting the Companion After Getting Out of the Car However, after the car arrived, the two Westerners jumped into the car, sat side by side, and chatted and laughed. Zhao was ordered to start the engine and drive west. They drove along Route Robert and Avenue Haig to the intersection of Lincoln Road and Warren Road. One of the Westerners ordered Zhao to stop the car. The two got out of the car one after another, pretending to talk as they walked eastward. One of them then pulled out a pistol from his pocket and fired two shots at the victim. One shot hit the victim's waist, and the other hit the victim's head. Both shots hit vital points, causing instant death. Blood was all over the ground. At that time, the driver Zhao Zhiming, witnessing the scene, was stunned and terrified in the car.

▲ Throwing the Body into the Creek Seeing that his purpose had been achieved, the murderer carried the body out of the car and ordered the driver to continue driving for about a mile. Then he ordered the driver to stop. The murderer jumped out of the car and threw the body into the creek there. He told the driver, "Don't be afraid. I'll take responsibility if anything happens." After saying this, the murderer walked away to the north.

▲ Detectives Went to Investigate Not long after, the driver Zhao Zhiliang, having recovered slightly from his shock, drove back at full speed and reported the situation to the foreman. The foreman immediately notified the Jing'an Temple Road Police Station by telephone. The police then sent detectives to investigate. It was verified that the deceased was wearing a light gray suit, was in his thirties, and had two gunshot wounds. The victim's yellow felt hat was taken back to the police station by the detectives for safekeeping. The body was sent to the morgue to await examination.

▲ The US Consulate is Investigating the Murderer According to investigations by reporters, the deceased was named R.K. Heim, and the murderer was his friend named T.M. Hansen. They were very good friends during their lifetime. Because they were unemployed in Shanghai, they were going to return to the United States together by ship. The cause of the murder has not yet been determined. The police station and the US Consulate are urgently arresting the murderer for punishment. It is reported that the murderer T.M. Hansen is the acting manager of Citibank in Tianjin. He had been in Shanghai for less than three days and lived in the Duchen Hotel on Simalu. The murdered R.K. Heim lived in the YMCA on Jing'an Temple Road and had previously worked in the same bank.

Sanitary Conditions in the Concession 171

▲ Free Injections to Prevent Cholera

At the Board of Directors meeting of the Public Works Department on the 15th of this month, the Director of the Health Department reported that the number of cholera cases had increased, but not as quickly as in previous epidemic years. This is the first time since 1902 that cholera has been discovered in May. It is impossible to know how extensive it will be this year, but fortunately, the rate of increase is not as dramatic as in 1902. Regarding the cleanliness of Zhabei, the Director stated that he had personally investigated it recently and that the situation was generally satisfactory. The first district has now been taken over by the Chinese authorities. There is some accumulation of garbage in this area, perhaps due to unavoidable oversights during the transition period. The second district is still being cleaned by the Public Works Department, and the situation is satisfactory. The Health Department is now increasing its equipment for free cholera injections. In addition to the injection car patrolling the concession, injections are given daily from 2:00 PM to 4:30 PM (except Saturdays and Sundays) at the following five health sub-offices: (Central District) 23 Hankou Road; (North District) 100 Qipu Road; (East District) 67 Huade Road; 10 Tongzhou Road; (West District) 28 Maigen Road. All Chinese and poor Westerners can go there.

Explanation of the Telephone Price Increase 178

Regarding the telephone price increase event announced by the Public Works Department yesterday, the phrase "Due to the fall in the price of silver, the company's capital expenditures have increased by 14% compared to Mr. Anstie's original estimate" in the original text is misleading. The so-called 14% increase is the amount of the increase in gold expenditure. If converted to silver, the amount of the increase is actually 117%. Mr. Anstie's original estimate was 8 million taels of silver, which at 2 shillings and 6.5 pence was converted to 4,936,000 yuan in gold. However, the company actually spent 5,636,229 yuan in gold, which is 14% more than the original estimate. In fact, due to the fall in the price of silver, 5,636,229 yuan in gold is equivalent to 17,342,242 taels of silver, which is more than double the original estimate of 8 million taels. The company's proposal was to first make Mr. Anstie's expenses applicable after implementation, and then increase the price by 11%. In this way, the company could obtain interest of about 6.7%. However, the Public Works Department is now only allowing Mr. Anstie's expenses to be changed to an applicable number. As for the additional increase, the company must submit a detailed explanation to the Public Works Departments of the two concessions and request their approval before it can be allowed.

Mr. Anstie's report stated, "In view of the company's needs in the coming years and the unfavorable exchange rate when importing equipment, it is proposed to temporarily allow the company to increase the price of commercial telephones from 78 taels to 105 taels, residential telephones from 52 taels to 65 taels, and private telephone lines from 40 to 50 taels per section, and extension lines and extensions by 25%... This price increase will increase the company's income by about one-quarter... but it is only a satisfactory method at present. The permanent price should be determined as soon as possible."

Article 13 of the company's franchise contract states, "The price list at the time of the contract should apply until the full conversion to automatic equipment, but the shareholders' price reduction method is not included in this example. After the full conversion to automatic equipment, the price should be agreed upon by the company and the Public Works Department. The standard should allow the company to obtain annual interest of 8%, plus an additional 2%. If the conversion to automatic equipment cannot be completed within two years, the price may not be increased during the period of delay, which is twice the duration of the two years. The annual net profit should be the total annual income, less maintenance costs, management fees, depreciation, stock raising funds, bad debts, insurance, pensions, savings, taxes, interest, and other expenses. However, stock interest, dividends, and business expansion reserve funds are not included. The company's business investment should include the following four items: (A) the paid-up capital and the excess income from the company's sale of shares; (B) the income from the issuance of bonds; (C) loans and mortgage loans, etc., with a term of more than one year, but overdrafts and outstanding accounts payable, etc., of a temporary nature, are not included; (D) general reserve fund, which is calculated based on the amount of capital used throughout the year."

Dinghai Fishermen Petition in Hangzhou 180

Daishan and Changtu Islands, under the jurisdiction of Dinghai County, are the most abundant fish-producing areas in our country. Even Sun Yat-sen's posthumous teachings in the National Reconstruction Strategy mentioned the idea of building a fishing port on Changtu Island to promote the long-term development of China's fishing industry. Therefore, in recent years, the National Government has spared no effort in reforming the administration of the fishing industry. In addition to abolishing the people-harming likin tax, it has also completely exempted fish taxes to demonstrate its dedication to revitalizing the fishing industry and benefiting the fishermen. Unexpectedly, while the government is striving for improvement and expansion, the two fish firms of Zha Pu Hongchang and Run Tai are taking advantage of the situation to monopolize, speculate, and exploit the fishermen, which is increasing day by day. This has aroused a serious backlash from all the fishermen on the two islands of the county, who are jointly seeking self-rescue. They have publicly elected Zhao Guohuang, Bao Zhenpin, and more than ten others to form a petition delegation responsible for representing the whole, and they have rushed to Nanjing and Hangzhou to present a petition to the Ministry of Industry and the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Construction, describing their oppressed situation and requesting relief. They are also asking for strict prohibition and suppression of the two firms' illegal acts of oppressing the fishermen. It is reported that the delegates passed through Shanghai yesterday on their way to Hangzhou. According to them, the fish firms have traditionally charged a commission of five per cent on the value of fish sold (i.e., five yuan commission for every hundred yuan), and another three per cent discount (i.e., three yuan commission for every hundred yuan). The combined commission and discount amount to eight yuan and fifty cents per hundred yuan, constituting a double commission exceeding one yuan. The fishermen believe that the discount is a form of fraud and express their dissatisfaction. However, due to the long-standing practice, they have had to endure it for the time being. Unexpectedly, the two firms have become even more unscrupulous and have added new abusive clauses. Since the spring of this year, they have jointly forced fishing boats to pass their accounts through Ningbo for fish sold in Zha Pu. If the fishermen take money on the spot in Zha Pu, they must charge three, four, five, or even six yuan per hundred yuan according to the current declared price in Ningbo, leaving it to the firms' consciences. This has turned into another double discount, with excessive amounts being deducted. Fishermen brave the dangers of wind and waves, risking their lives in the ocean to catch fish and support their families. After a year of hard work, the meager profits they earn are now being heavily exploited by the two firms, making it unbearable for the fishermen. Therefore, as a last resort, they have publicly elected representatives to go to Nanjing and Zhejiang to appeal and request strict prohibition of the firms' illegal activities, the recovery of overcharged amounts, and the relief of the suffering of the majority of fishermen. Fortunately, the Ministry of Industry has approved the case and instructed the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Construction to investigate and handle it in detail. Therefore, the delegates urgently need to petition in Hangzhou in order to achieve the goal of severely punishing the illegal acts of the two firms and recovering the overcharged funds, thus relieving the suffering of the majority of fishermen.

Great China 185

Donggou Splint Factory Electricity

▲ Supplied by Pudong Electric Company

Great China Match Company has been quite developed in business recently. There is a splint factory in Donggou, Pudong, which is large in scale and well managed. It is the giant of the national self-run match splint factory, equipped with a 120-horsepower steam engine and generator. The electric lights and power required by the factory are all supplied by its own machine. Later, after calculating the cost of coal, wages, repairs, etc., the expenses were huge and uneconomical, and the management was complicated and inconvenient. The capacity was limited and could not be expanded arbitrarily. However, the Pudong Electric Company has abundant power, supplies it day and night, and charges are cheap, which is more cost-effective. Therefore, the factory has now stopped its own machine and completely switched to the electricity supply of Pudong Electric Company. It is said that the monthly power cost can be saved a lot.

It is hoped that all circles, in view of Mr. Wang's concern for the bones and his painstaking efforts, will be willing to support this righteous cause.

Robbery and Assault on Guohuo Road 192

▲ None of the Robbers Have Been Apprehended

▲ The Injured Person May Become Disabled

The bean sprout workshop opened by Pan Huayun, a Shaoxing native, at No. 28 Yunjili, behind the Shanghai-Minhang South Extension Long-Distance Bus Company on Guohuo Road in the South City, has a fairly good business, which is coveted by robbers. The night before last, Pan was attending a Guandi gathering and drinking alcohol. He took out all the cash and silver dollars at home to be used, so there was no cash in the house. Unexpectedly, at around 9:00 PM, four robbers suddenly came, two wearing long black gowns and two wearing short blue cloth shirts and pants, each holding a handgun. When they arrived at Pan's house, only Pan's wife, Mrs. Pan Xu, and two infants were at home, already asleep. The robbers went forward and pushed the door open. The neighbor, Mrs. Zhu Wang, was holding a child and standing at the door. When the robbers saw her, they immediately watched her. Seeing that she had a pair of gold rings, they slapped her twice on the face and took the rings. They immediately went to Pan's house and forbade her from making any noise. Although they robbed the house, they only got a pair of silver bracelets, a silver lock piece, a cloud gauze shirt, a blue cloth shirt, a straw hat, and a felt hat. At that time, the child saw it and cried loudly, and the sound was heard outside. The robbers stopped and fled with what they had robbed. The two women also went out. Many Shaoxing natives lived nearby. After learning about it, they each grabbed shoulder poles and bamboo poles and chased after the robbers. When they arrived on Guohuo Road, the smoke and paper store sounded the alarm whistle, and the bandits fled east. Seeing the sound of the alarm and the pursuers behind them, they fired their guns randomly and ran to the South Mountain Lane entrance, which was more than twenty houses away. A coppersmith nicknamed "Little Pockmark" (a Shaoxing native) had just walked out of the lane. Seeing this situation, he did not know it was a robbery and ran to the road to watch. The robbers fired at him, and one bullet hit Little Pockmark's right leg, penetrated his left leg, and then entered his right leg again, getting stuck in the bone. Little Pockmark was injured in both feet and fell to the ground, unable to stand up. The robbers continued to fire their guns and fled east towards the Shanghai Military Camp. None of the robbers were caught. Therefore, the robbed person admitted that he was unlucky, and the injured person was taken to the Shanghai Hospital by his wife to be treated after reporting to the police station in the Second District, fearing that he would become disabled.

Inauguration of the Directors and Supervisors of the Lianyi Society of the Transportation Department of the French Concession Water and Electricity Company 193

The newly elected directors and supervisors of the Lianyi Society of the Transportation Department of the French Concession Water and Electricity Company, located at 244 Avenue Foch, held a swearing-in ceremony at 6:00 PM on the 15th. Immediately afterwards, the first joint meeting of directors and supervisors was held. (A) Reports, omitted. (5) The meeting adjourned.

Appeal of the Hadong Tenants' Association 194

▲ Three Demands

The Hadong Tenants' Association in this city has raised three reasons to the landlord, including correcting the lunar calendar for rent collection, reducing wartime rent, and reducing rent in response to the market downturn. They have not been accepted. They have filed appeals to the city's party and government organs, commercial associations, city unions, and various groups, requesting them to uphold fairness. The original text reads: "[The members of the association, etc., have rented Hadong's houses for many years. On January 28th this year, the Japanese army invaded the city, and the market was closed for two months, causing extreme hardship. Therefore, they wrote to the owner, Madam Luo Jialing, asking her to voluntarily waive the wartime rent, reduce the rent rate in the future, and correct the bad habit of collecting rent according to the lunar calendar, so as to conform to the law and alleviate the difficulties of the merchants, preserve the vitality after the war, and look forward to the prosperity of society. Unexpectedly, two letters were sent, but no reply was received. The merchants were deeply disappointed. Unexpectedly, things did not end there. The Hadong Foreign Company not only ignored the requirements of the association, but also used its position and power to wantonly destroy. Recently, for example, the Lianli Huazhuangpin Company in Huajin Lane, due to the impact of the war, owed five months' rent. It repeatedly stated that it would pay three months first, but the rental office refused to accept it and instead fabricated reasons to provide a guarantee in the special district court, applying to put the company under temporary detention. Also, if the Xiangmao Silk Thread Company on Er Malu retained and deferred payment of the February and March rent according to the city's reduction principle, it unexpectedly angered the rental office, which again used the excuse of renovating the house and taking it back for its own use, and applied to the court for temporary enforcement. Also, if the Taikang Company was elected by the public as one of the executive committee members due to the establishment of the association, the rental office held a grudge in its heart. On the afternoon of the 15th, it led ten people to the company in the name of collecting rent, roaring and coercing. Such incidents are countless. The association's various demands to the owner this time are not unreasonable, but the owner did not examine them carefully and instead trampled on them, which made the association feel regret and pain. As a last resort, the association had to appeal to your bureau for fair assistance for various demands and reasons. (1) Correcting the lunar calendar for rent collection: Shanghai is a part of the territory of the Republic of China, and the national laws should be obeyed by all. Since the national government ordered the abolition of the lunar calendar, all merchants, whether Chinese or foreign, have long complied with the reform for rent, but Hadong still relies on its power and continues to collect rent according to the lunar calendar, violating government laws and exploiting the interests of tenants. One who should immediately correct the government order. (2) Reducing and exempting rent during the war period: Since the outbreak of the Sino-Japanese War, not only February and March were during the shutdown period, suffering great losses, but even April and May, although the market has nominally opened, the business situation is much worse than before. It is like a weak body after illness, and it is necessary to reduce its burden in order to recover it as soon as possible. The rent for February and March should be reduced and exempted. Two (3) Implementing automatic rent reduction: The rent of Hadong's houses is the highest in the city. Taking the market houses in the San Malu area as an example, due to the high rent, no one dares to ask. The market houses have been closed for more than a year and are all eyesores. The same location, the same form, used to rent for more than one hundred taels per house, but now it rents for only eighty taels or seventy-five taels per house. From this example, how much do old tenants lose compared to new tenants? The Hadong Foreign Company always raises the rent whenever the market is slightly prosperous, but never reduces the rent when the market declines. Considering the current market decline, the rent should be reduced. Three. In summary, the above three are all legitimate demands that cannot be delayed. I sincerely request your bureau to understand the difficulties of the merchants, take on the role of mediation, and also issue an official letter to the special district court, paying attention to the suffering of the merchants, and not approving applications for temporary enforcement and temporary detention. I am eagerly awaiting orders.]"

Achievements of the Famous Doctor Wang Jiyan 198

Wang Jiyan, a famous doctor from Huizhou, who traveled to Wuhu, has been invited to Shanghai and retained by famous and prestigious figures. Since he temporarily resided in Jinfuli at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Datong Road, those who came to seek medical treatment were all long-term, difficult, and serious cases, such as asthma, cough, hemoptysis, liver and stomach bloating, flatulence, consumptive labor, flaccidity, seminal emission, abnormal menstruation in women, menstrual pain, metrorrhagia, band pain, masses, infertility, etc. All of them can have immediate magical effects. The most magical thing is the case of a certain Mr. Xi, whose chest and abdomen were oppressed as if bound for more than three years. He had taken more than 500 doses of medicine, and previous doctors all thought it was a stomach disease. Only Mr. Wang diagnosed it as a tumor on the inner wall of the chest cavity. After taking more than a dozen doses of medicine, it gradually shrunk. The patient himself began to feel as if there was something binding on the inner chest wall. Mr. Wang received a high-level scientific education and was later taught by famous teachers. He was proficient in pulse theory and had rich experience. In the past ten years, he has made some inventions in the field of Chinese medicine, which is truly rare in the Chinese medical community.

Comments

Don't Be Like a Fool Waiting for the Sky to Fall 218

— Buddha

According to foreign sources yesterday, the Soviet Union is very cold towards the Sino-Russian resumption of diplomatic relations talks, which further shows that Japan and Russia have already exchanged opinions. Our side is not without lagging behind. If this situation continues, then the previous talks were unfortunately correct.

Although the authorities regard the issue of Sino-Russian resumption of diplomatic relations as important, we do not regard it as important. The authorities regard it as disappointing, but we do not regard it as disappointing. The fact that weak countries have no diplomacy is an iron rule like a mountain. Even if the Soviet Union and our country really resume diplomatic relations, it is difficult to predict what the effect will be, and there are many issues that should be considered after the resumption of diplomatic relations, and it is not certain that any benefits will be received.

[If the fence is broken, stray dogs will drill in]. We should repair the fence first, then stray dogs will naturally have no way to enter. Now, without repairing the fence first, we are eagerly hoping for the鹬蚌之爭(snipe and clam fight) and reaping the fisherman's profits. It is really [like a fool waiting for the sky to fall, a poor man waiting for the people to rebel]. Its foolishness is unmatched. I look back and look at our country's politics, party affairs, military affairs, and industry. There is nothing that does not make people sigh and feel pessimistic.

There is a saying: "Heaven's sins can be violated, but one's own sins cannot be lived."

Literature & Art

Wandering Along the Bund Park on a Rainy Night 219

— Meng Zhaozhuan Master

After the disaster, I searched for the pavilions in order, and the old gardens and forests are still outside the world. In the rain, the light of the lamps sinks in thousands of halos, and the sound of cars accompanies a chant under the leaves. Sitting and feeling that the river flows without a fixed form, I temporarily collect my soul and merge with the layers of shade. I wait for the moon and peek at the stars, striving to sink and float together with the Divine Land.

Composed on the Returning Car Passing Through the Battlefield 220

—

The carriage dream carries ten thousand thunders, passing through hundreds of villages in the sound of plum rain. After the disaster, the wind and flowers are so old, and to whom can I warm the liver and gallbladder in my heart? I imagine the rivers and mountains as a battle of dragons, and a crane returns from the sky and the sea. I cannot finish listening to the cries of thousands of families in the wilderness, and Jiangnan still has souls that have not been summoned.

Science

Making Canned Food at Home 221

— Jing Yu

There are countless microorganisms breeding in the air. Food such as fish and meat will rot if left for a long time due to their erosion. Therefore, to avoid this problem, it is necessary to use canning methods.

Storing things in cans is the canned food sold on the market. Because canned food is successfully manufactured using scientific methods, the air and all microorganisms in the can are eliminated completely. It can be preserved for a long time and will never spoil. However, although there are many canned food companies in Shanghai, the manufacturing methods rely entirely on machinery, which is not easily imitated in the home. Therefore, in order to travel outside and be convenient to carry, one can only buy products from various companies on the market. However, the various products of various companies are all the same, which is already a defect. Moreover, their products cannot have all the dishes that home-cooked dishes should have, which is even more difficult to satisfy the appetite of general gourmets. There is now a homemade method that has been proven through practice and the results are excellent. If readers can follow it, it will be easy to carry the dishes they like to eat every day. Even if traveling to foreign countries, the flavor of their hometown can still please my taste buds. Then, even when I am in a foreign land, it is no different from my hometown, so why not do it? Now, I will disclose it as follows, please try it.

After eating the canned food you bought, do not discard the cans. Wait until you have accumulated a lot, wash them one by one, and dry the water stains. If the can surface is broken, find another piece of tinplate and cut it to the appropriate size according to the diameter of the can. After you cook the things you like to eat, put them into the cans one by one, add the can surface, and seal it with tin. Then put the cans into the pot, add water to half of the can, and cook it over high heat for about half an hour to make the contents of the can boil and emit steam. Take the can out, and use a drill to drill a small hole in the can surface. Once the drill is pulled out, immediately use tin to plug the hole. At this point, the procedure is complete, and the canned food has been successfully made. Because the tinplate on the can surface is just drilled through, you can hear a sound. At the moment of this sound, all the air sealed in the can and the remaining microorganisms are squeezed out by the steam, leaving nothing. In this way, it can be kept permanently and has the same effect as mechanically made ones.

Student Writing

Elementary School Students' Prank 222

— Kai Tao

[Hey! Mr. Niu is here! Ha! Ha! Mr. Niu is here! ...]

Many students shouted arrogantly. It turned out that the class bell had already rung. On the top of Mr. Niu's [Chinese teacher's] hat, the students had already added a chopstick-like white paper strip. Moreover, he was wearing a pair of old glasses and an old bamboo cloth long gown, walking towards the classroom with sweat all over his face. Of course, how could the fashionable and nosy students not laugh?

Lu and Ma, students who were famous for being cunning, saw that the teacher had not yet approached, so they used their magical abilities and hurriedly put the blackboard-wiping cloth on the half-open classroom door, preparing to let the teacher taste it. Now, all the students in the hall were as silent as if they had taken a sedative tonic, sitting silently.

Mr. Niu had always walked in slowly, but today he was late because he had something to do, so he rushed forward, regardless of everything, and pushed the door open. Who knew that his apprentice's sky-falling prop had hit him down, scaring the old man out of his wits. He shouted, [Yo!], and the old glasses had already unfortunately been shattered into pieces. Mr. Niu then launched a punitive expedition.

[Which fool?] Mr. Niu said angrily.

The students were all silent. Mr. Niu went to report to the principal, but the chopstick strip was still waving on Mr. Niu's head as he thought secretly,

[Are my eyes okay! ...]

Five Acts

New Maritime Scam 223

— Wu Jichen

[More people than positions] [It is difficult to find a job] These two sentences are the biggest obstacles in the lifeline. When unemployed people have no way to be recommended and wander around, they have to look for opportunities in the newspapers every day. Every day there are people asking for staff and seeking cooperation, but the result is still disappointing, because most of them require hundreds or even dozens of yuan in guarantee money in exchange for a job. Just imagine, how can poor unemployed people afford this ability to bear?

My friend Mr. Zhang is also one of the unemployed. One day he saw an advertisement in the × newspaper, which said:

Recruiting Male and Female Actors

Entrusted by major famous film companies, dozens of male and female actors are being recruited. Those who want to appear on the silver screen, regardless of age, only need to be literate. There is a price of 50 cents to 1 yuan per day. This is a rare opportunity, so register as soon as possible. No fees are charged for registration. Registration location: ×× Lane ×× Road ×× Number, Shanghai ×× Film Company

This kind of opportunity that does not require a guarantee or fees is indeed rare. Mr. Zhang enthusiastically joined. Who knew that the address of the so-called ×× Film Company was a stove shop in ×× Lane. The characters inside were very beautiful and dressed in Western clothes. Everything was arranged except for a broken desk and three or four wooden chairs, and a few star photos nailed on the wall with pictures. Nothing valuable could be found. Their advertisement clearly stated that no fees would be charged, but when joining, they had to pay a registration fee of 60 cents and a handling fee of 40 cents. Because the amount was still small, it was really difficult to find a job, and most of the people who registered did not argue with them. At that time, they paid up. On the third day, they really set off to ×× Company to participate in the filming of ××××. Every morning, a car from ×× Company came to pick them up and returned them at night. Food and lodging were all prepared by themselves. After about a dozen times of filming, the director of the company said that the filming of ×× Company's film was completed. Please go home and rest for two days, and he will calculate and pay the wages before filming again. So we happily went home and waited quietly for two days. When we went to ×× Film Company again, it was already empty!

Family Problems

Dowry 224

— He Zhou

When Mrs. Zhang married her eldest son five years ago, she was very dissatisfied because the "dowry" brought by her daughter-in-law was very meager. For this reason, she spoke about it repeatedly in front of people; "It cost so much money to marry a poor woman, it's really not worth it!" Although this eldest daughter-in-law was very capable and filial to her, she still couldn't win Mrs. Zhang's favor. Even the maids secretly said; "Isn't the eldest grandma as poor as us?" Some even said; "No wonder the wife doesn't like her."

Recently, Mrs. Zhang married a second daughter-in-law. Needless to say, when she arranged the engagement for her son, the first condition she asked was "Is the woman's family rich and powerful?" The matchmaker praised her in every possible way; "The woman's family is really rich. Her father owns two large pawnshops and four foreign goods stores, making a lot of money every year. Several of her brothers-in-law all work in banks." This made Mrs. Zhang so happy that the marriage was settled in one go.

That was not a lie. On the day the second son got married, the Zhang family was filled with joy and the sound of drums and music filled the sky. The new daughter-in-law's "dowry" was indeed rich and plentiful, filling three or four moving trucks. A room was filled with colorful brocades, almost all of which were precious things, attracting people to watch and admire them. Mrs. Zhang felt that she had been blessed by heaven.

After the second grandma married in, Mrs. Zhang naturally loved her very much. She always took her with her when she went to restaurants and theaters. But what about the eldest grandma? She could never enjoy this favor, but she understood very well; "This is because the daughter of a poor family cannot afford a rich "dowry"." Alas! The daughters of poor families have such unspeakable pain when they marry as daughters-in-law.

Business Economics

The Lesson of the Pancake Shop 225

— Gui

Behind our school, on a street, there are two pancake shops, facing each other. Initially, their business scale and the pancakes they made were all on the same level.

But the situation has changed recently.

Shop A has recently been improved, adding many varieties, such as lard pancakes, ham pancakes, etc. The taste is really much better than before. Moreover, white sugar mixed with red and green silk, red ham, green onions, and white lard are placed in snow-white basins and displayed on the table. The form has also improved a lot, and the business is developing rapidly.

Shop B, however, remains the same, sticking to the old ways. The original customers have been attracted to Shop A. The unclean pancakes and fried dough sticks are unattended. Its boss stares at the opposite peer with jealousy and envy. Obviously, Shop A has developed due to improvement, and Shop B has been eliminated due to conservatism.

From small to large, the way of business is like this. Especially in the modern and fiercely competitive business field, we must strive for improvement.

Nonsense

Maintaining the Lunar Calendar 226

— Shui Ye

On the day of the abolished Dragon Boat Festival, a cement alley was filled with the aroma of rice dumplings. Many children had the character "king" written on their foreheads, and many children were wearing yellow tiger clothes. They had smiles on their faces because it was a happy day. Two × officials came from afar, carrying empty briefcases on their backs. They stopped at a door and said to the people inside, "The Dragon Boat Festival is here. Thank you. Give us some money for wine." The people inside said, "The lunar calendar has been abolished. Why are you still asking for money on the holiday?" The two of them said calmly, "We are not abolishing the lunar calendar, we are maintaining it." The owner gave them 20 cents, both as a reward for their usual help and to maintain the already abolished lunar calendar.

Bamboo Elegant Fragments

Terminalia 227

— Song Lu

In the literary column of this journal a few days ago, I read a bamboo branch poem by Zhang Gongyu about women. The original poem is like this:

"Cicada clothes lean against arms, revealing creamy chest, short hair, black threads, curling and unkempt; the most soul-stirring place is the gully, deeply hidden terminalia on the two high peaks."

"Terminalia", this term, it seems that some people not only do not understand its allusion, but also may not understand its explanation, so I will give it a textual research.

It turns out that this allusion comes from the Anecdotes of the Tang Palace. The general facts are like this:

"Yang Guifei had an affair with An Lushan. An mistakenly scratched the Consort's breast with his claws. The Consort cried and said: "It is my fault to have an affair with you!" Fearing that the Emperor would see it, she embroidered a chest cover to cover it, and named it terminalia."

In this way, terminalia is a women's chest-hugging embroidered garment, which is the so-called "bodice". If it is compared with modern costumes, it is also the role of a small vest.

Originally, the binding of women's chests was a bad habit. This custom may not have existed before the Tang Dynasty? The one who created this was Yang Guifei, and the reason why Yang Guifei did this is also laughable, because she was scratched on the nipple by An Lushan, and she used this to deceive Emperor Ming. Then, as customs continued, this trend was actually imitating Yang Guifei's actions. To put it bluntly, it can't help but make people laugh.

Since the past few years, the voice of promoting breast-release has been expanding day by day. The small vest has been overthrown. Many modern women, with their towering peaks hidden on their chests, swagger through the market, with great seduction, which makes general moral scholars criticize it as "related to the morality of lewdness." Although I am an extreme supporter of the breast-release movement, after seeing that kind of "fleshy seduction", I can't help but regard the advocacy of big breasts and the reform of clothing as problems that need to be studied urgently.

Due to space limitations, this article will be put on hold for now. If there is an opportunity, I will write another article to discuss women's clothing.

▲Public Notice▲

Public Notice regarding the Delivery of Litigation Documents:

All fees that this court collects from parties for the delivery of litigation documents by court clerks are clearly marked with the amount due on the documents. Fees are collected accordingly, and a receipt is issued as proof. No extra fees are allowed whatsoever. This has been the practice for a long time. However, we fear that over time, the court clerks may become complacent and take the matter lightly, or that some may still solicit additional payments from the parties. Strict prevention is necessary to reduce litigation burdens. Therefore, this notice is issued. If, in the future, any parties encounter court clerks soliciting additional payments, they may immediately report the names of the clerks to the court. Upon verification, strict punishment will be imposed without leniency. Please take note of this.

Zhou Xianjue, Head of the Court

June 17, 1932, Republic of China

Cao Youpeng is sentenced to six months imprisonment for the crime of theft by breaking through a wall. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be credited at a rate of one day of imprisonment for every two days of detention.

Police Department v. Li Saizi Opium Case (Verdict): 284

Li Saizi is fined 50 yuan for the crime of possessing a special opium substitute. If the fine is converted to imprisonment, one day of imprisonment will be substituted for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be credited at a rate of two yuan of the fine for every day of detention. Two small bags of red pills (weighing half a pound each) will be confiscated.

Police Department v. Tao'er Qigaofu Embezzlement Case (Verdict): 285

Tao'er Qigaofu is fined 10 yuan for the crime of embezzlement. If unable to pay, one day of imprisonment will be substituted for every two yuan.

Police Department v. Lu Genlin et al. Theft Case (Verdict): 286

Lu Genlin and Lu Hailin are each sentenced to ten days detention for the crime of joint theft. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be credited at a rate of one day of detention for every two days of detention. (June 16th)
